# CLAUDE.md Рђћ BLOOM project agent context

This file is the contract between the project and any AI agent working on it. Read it at the start of every session. Update it whenever the project changes Рђћ see [Living docs rule](#living-docs-rule) at the bottom.

The human-facing description lives in [README.md](README.md). This file focuses on what an AI needs to continue work without re-reading the entire codebase.

---

## ­ЪЌ║№ИЈ Retention Stages Tracker (May 2026, updated 2026-05-23)

Quick-scan map of the addiction-loop work. **Update this table whenever a stage ships.** Detailed change-log entries live in ┬Д11 below.

### РюЁ Completed stages (post-roadmap retention layer)
| # | Stage | Surface |
|---|---|---|
| 1 | **FOMO countdown** | Home button + picker cards show `­ЪћЦ ОъОАОфОЎОЎОЮ ОЉОбОЋОЊ 4ОЕ`. Loss-aversion. |
| 2 | **Per-board personal best** | `­ЪЈє ОюОбОЉОЋОе: 47K (ОљОфОћ)` chip; live-swap to `­ЪЉЉ ОбОЉОеОф!` mid-game. |
| 3 | **Global per-board leaderboard** | `­ЪЉЉ ОЊОаОЎОљОю: 89K` chip; rank pill on game-over (`#3 / 87 ┬и ОбОЉОеОф 95%`). |
| 4 | **Top-50 leaderboard modal** | Per-board trophy Рєњ modal with podium + "you" row + "next-to-beat" target. |
| 5 | **Cross-board streak** | `­ЪћЦ ОеОдОБ N ОЎОъОЎОЮ ┬и ОбОЋОЊ M ОюОЉОљОЊОњ'` with 6 milestones (50Рєњ2000­Ъњј). |
| 6 | **Achievements** | 5 per-board + 6 cross-board badges (25Рєњ1000­Ъњј); modal catalog. |
| 7 | **Daily quests** | 3 deterministic-per-day quests, manual claim (Clash Royale hook). |
| 7.5 | **Full admin control** | 34 new config keys: 6 master toggles + 28 per-reward (quests/ach/streak). |
| 8 | **Mystery Chest (Skinner box)** | Slot-machine reveal after every dynamic game; 5 rarity tiers + pity. |
| 9 | **Streak Freeze + Comeback** | ­ЪЏА Duolingo-style insurance + ­ЪЉІ ОЉОеОЋОџ ОЕОЋОЉОџ overlay for lapsed players. |
| 10 | **Push Notifications** | Admin broadcast UI + smart prompts at first streak/ach/comeback. |
| ­ЪљЏ | **Critical bug-fix** | `updated_at` column missing Рєњ 500 fix; reward-clamp bypass for quest/ach/streak (paid 10­Ъњј instead of N­Ъњј); shop +2 items. |
| **11** | **Season Pass** РГљ | 20-tier Battle-Pass with XP from every action; manual claim per tier (16K­Ъњј/season). |
| **12** | **Live Tournaments** ­ЪЈє | Scheduled prime-time events with top-N prize pool + auto-finalize + push to winners. |
| **13** | **Friends invite + shared streak** ­ЪЉЦ | Viral: invite via WhatsApp Рєњ both get 200­Ъњј; shared-play days Рєњ +100­Ъњј each. |
| **14** | **Daily-login ├Ќ streak multiplier** ­ЪјЂ | Daily bonus shows breakdown rows: base ├Ќ streak ├Ќ dyn-streak ├Ќ friend-shared. Locked rows = prospective FOMO. |
| **15** | **Daily mini-event boards** ­ЪїЪ | Deterministic per-day pick of "­ЪїЪ ОћОюОЋОЌ ОЕОю ОћОЎОЋОЮ" with ├Ќ3 XP + ├Ќ2 quest rewards. Gold-pink banner at top of picker + special card glow + home FOMO label + game-over celebration. |
| **G1-G4** | **UX gaps fix + monetization roadmap** | Dedicated admin Battle Pass + Daily Special panels; Battle Pass on home as primary tile; [BLOOM_MONETIZATION_ROADMAP.md](BLOOM_MONETIZATION_ROADMAP.md) with stages 17-32. |
| **17** | **Premium Battle Pass** Рюе | Dual-track Battle Pass Рђћ purchase ├Ќ2 rewards per tier for 1500­Ъњј (or $4.99 IAP, display only). Locked-but-earned premium rewards visually show as ­Ъћњ to drive loss-aversion. Atomic buy + dual-track claim. The #1 monetization driver. |
| **20** | **Starter Pack** ­ЪјЂ | First-purchase funnel Рђћ fires after player crosses 5K score for the first time. 7-day countdown + one-time-only. 500­Ъњј Рєњ 1500­Ъњј + skin + 3 BP tiers (5├Ќ ROI). Loud gold-pink banner at top of home + big modal. The single highest-conversion offer in F2P puzzle games (50-90% buy-through). |
| **21** | **Daily Deals** ­ЪћЦ | One rotating deal per day (Asia/Jerusalem). 7 seeded deals: gem packs, skin deal, BP boost, chest x3, freeze x3, mega bundle. Anchoring psychology ("ОЌОАОЏОф 60%!"). Red-orange pulsing banner on home + modal with live countdown. One-purchase-per-day-per-deal. Daily-return hook. |
| **18** | **Skin Gacha** ­Ъј░ | The Genshin/Apex pattern. 5 rarity tiers (common 60% Рєњ mythic 0.5%) + 50-pull pity + **daily free pull** + 10x bundle with 10% discount + featured-item boost. Full animated reveal sequence with rolling orb Рєњ card pop Рєњ rarity-themed glow. Seeded with 17 pool entries. Duplicates auto-convert to gems at 50%. The variable-reward Skinner box that drives $4B/year in F2P cosmetics. |
| **19** | **Lives / Energy** РЮц№ИЈ | Candy Crush pattern (DEFAULT-OFF, admin opt-in). 5 lives, regen 1/30min, refill via ad / 50­Ъњј / wait. Applies ONLY to dynamic boards (daily/practice/contests/duels/challenges stay unlimited). Hearts widget on home with live countdown. Out-of-lives modal with 3 refill paths. Controversial Рђћ can boost retention OR cause uninstalls. A/B-test gated. |
| **26** | **Live Ops Calendar + Daily Checklist** ­ЪЊЁ | Two surfaces: (1) Daily Checklist tile on home Рђћ 5 to-do items (free gacha pull, daily special, daily deal, quest, streak) with progress bar; completionist drive Рђћ Clash Royale pattern reports +25% DAU. (2) Full 30-day calendar modal aggregating tournaments + daily specials + season end + custom admin events; plan-ahead anchoring. Custom events CRUD via admin. |
| **28** | **Pet / Mascot** ­Ъї▒ | Tamagotchi pattern Рђћ a flower pet that grows with the player. 4 evolution stages (­Ъї▒Рєњ­Ъї┐Рєњ­ЪїИРєњ­Ъї║) + 4 moods (­ЪўіРєњ­ЪўљРєњ­ЪўбРєњ­ЪўГ) by time-since-visit. 2 daily actions: ­ЪњЌ pet (free, +20­Ъњј/day) + ­ЪЇй feed (10­ЪњјРєњ50XP, max 3/day). Pet XP also auto-grants from every game. Emotional anchor with guilt-trip mechanic Рђћ sad/crying pet pulses red on home. The pattern that built a $10B Tamagotchi industry by itself. |
| **25** | **Limited-time Bundles** ­ЪјЂ | Themed multi-day event packs (Hanukkah/Valentine/Black Friday). Per-bundle theme color + floating decoration emojis in the modal. Live countdown + scarcity ("only 1 per device"). 3 admin presets (one-click create). 3 seeded sample bundles. Stronger FOMO than Daily Deals because the window is 3-30 days (anticipation builds). |
| **16** | **Achievement-driven Cross-Leaderboard** ­ЪЈЁ | NEW competitive axis Рђћ global rank by # achievements unlocked (not score). Rewards completionists / breadth-players over single-board grinders. Boot syncs localStorage achievements to server via bulk POST. Home tile shows my count + global rank (only if 3+). Modal with top 50 + my-rank pill. Admin: top-20 view. |
| **29** | **Tile Collection Album** ­ЪЊћ | Genshin-style visual collection Рђћ 8 tiers ├Ќ N dynamic boards grid. Each game-over auto-records the highest tier reached. 2 reward axes: **board complete** (all 8 tiers on one board = 500­Ъњј) + **tier complete** (same tier on all boards = 200­Ъњј). Atomic claim. Indigo-teal album modal with collected/locked cell visuals, progress bars per tier-row, claim buttons. |
| **30** | **Lifetime Progression** РГљ | Call of Duty Prestige pattern Рђћ NEVER resets between seasons. XP **computed automatically** from aggregate of existing activity (games├Ќ10 + achievements├Ќ75 + gems-earned├и2 + album├Ќ25 + gacha├Ќ5 + pet-level├Ќ50 + BP-tier├Ќ100 + friends├Ќ200). No new XP grants needed Рђћ existing players are rewarded retroactively. Levels 1-100 Рєњ Prestige РГљ (max 10 stars = 5000­Ъњј each). Deep purple-gold theme. The longest meta-arc in the game. |
| **31** | **Smart Notifications** ­Ъцќ | Auto-scheduler scans subscribed devices every 30 min (9-22 ОЕОбОЋОЪ ОЎОЕОеОљОю only), picks the highest-emotion signal per device, sends ONE personalized push. 8 signals ranked: ­Ъўб pet crying > ­ЪЈє tournament ending > ­ЪЉЦ friend played > ­ЪћЦ streak danger > ­Ъјќ BP unclaimed > ­ЪЉІ comeback > ­ЪїЪ daily special > daily play. 12h cooldown. Stage 10 broadcast still works for "send to everyone". |
| **32** | **Replay Sharing** ­ЪЊц | K-factor viral lever. Game-over with score above threshold shows pulsing pink-purple "­ЪЊц ОЕОфОБ ОљОф ОћОаОЎОдОЌОЋОЪ ОЕОюОџ" button. Click Рєњ modal with 9:16 canvas-rendered PNG (gradient bg, big score, tier emoji, challenge text, branding+URL) + 4 share buttons (­Ъњг WhatsApp, ­ЪЊц Native, ­ЪЊІ Copy, ­ЪњЙ Save). Pre-filled text with `{score}`/`{url}` placeholders + "ОаОАОћ ОюОЕОЉОЋОе ОљОЋОфОЎ" challenge psychology. Every shared replay = potential new user. Admin telemetry: top sharers + breakdown by channel. |
| **27** | **Guilds / Clans** ­ЪЏА | Peer-pressure retention Рђћ industry data: +35% D30, 3.4├Ќ sessions/day vs solo. Create-or-join (500­Ъњј to create, 6-char codes), up to 30 members per clan. **Daily collective goal**: 30 crowns together Рєњ each member can claim 200­Ъњј reward. Auto-contribute from game-over scans the grid for crowns. Member leaderboard inside the modal shows who's pulling the most weight. Royal blue + gold theme. Toast notifications for contributions + goal-complete celebrations. |
| **33** | **Rivalry System** ­ЪЦі | Auto-paired 24h personal competition. Scheduler runs every 4h, finds players close in lifetime XP (within 10%), creates reciprocal rivalries. Home tile shows opponent's name + delta + countdown. **Behind = red pulse, ahead = gold celebration**. Win by gaining more XP in 24h Рєњ +150­Ъњј. Clash Royale pattern Рђћ personal beats abstract LB. |
| **34** | **Weekly Leagues** Рџћ№ИЈ | 5-tier ladder (­ЪЦЅBronze Рєњ ­ЪЉЉMaster) based on Lifetime XP gained THIS week. Sunday weekly reset (Asia/Jerusalem) via lazy-init snapshot. Each tier = end-of-week reward (50/150/400/1000/3000­Ъњј). Brawl Stars pattern that adds week-over-week competitive structure absent before. Promotion celebrations + home tile with progress to next tier. |
| **35** | **Home Variants A/B** ­ЪЈа | Admin picks 1 of 4 home layouts for ALL players: ­ЪЊ║ **standard** (current v2) / ­Ъја **carousel** (top "what's hot" scroll) / ­Ъј» **hero** (massive single-action card + collapse rest behind expander) / ­ЪјЊ **jit** (Just-In-Time Рђћ tiles unlock progressively by games played with ­ЪјЅ celebrations). Decorator pattern layered on top of v2 Рђћ each tile's own logic untouched. Configurable JIT unlock thresholds (default 3/7/13/26 games). |
| **36** | **Daily Spin Wheel** ­ЪјА | Coin Master pattern Рђћ single most addictive daily-return mechanic in F2P puzzles ($1B/year industry). 12-segment SVG wheel with weighted random server-rolled rewards (gems 10-1000, BP XP, streak freeze, mystery chest, jackpot 5000­Ъњј). 4.2s deceleration spin animation with tick sounds. Streak bonus (+10%/day, cap +200%) for consecutive-day spinners. Atomic server transaction. Home tile in purple-gold gradient with breathing pulse when available. Integrated into all 4 home variants (top priority in Hero + first card in Carousel). |
| **37** | **Guild Wars** ­ЪЏАРџћ№ИЈ | Clash Royale pattern Рђћ clan-vs-clan weekly competition. Boosted guild retention 3-5x at Supercell's launch. Auto-matchmaker runs every 6h, pairs eligible guilds (3+ members, no active war) by power level. 7-day war period. Every member's game score contributes to their guild's war pool via the existing `/guilds/contribute` endpoint (zero client wiring Рђћ extended server-side). End of war: lazy-finalize on next state read Рєњ winner gets 500­Ъњј/member + push notification, loser gets 100­Ъњј/member consolation. Min 1 game played to claim. Home tile (purple gradient Рєњ gold when reward unclaimed) only mounts when in-guild + has active war OR unclaimed reward. Modal: VS card with both teams' scores + progress bar + countdown, top-10 contributors leaderboard, my-contribution stats. Atomic gem credit + claim-dedup transaction. |
| **38** | **Trophy Road** ­ЪЈє | The #1 retention mechanism in mobile games (Clash Royale, Brawl Stars). Unlike League/BP, **trophies can GO DOWN**. Win (РЅЦ500 score) = +15­ЪЈє (+40 crown / +25 PB bonus). Lose (<100 score) = Рѕњ8­ЪЈє. New-player protection: under 50­ЪЈє = no loss. Safe floor at 0. 8 visual arenas (­Ъї▒ sprout Рєњ РџА legend at 12000) + 10 admin-tunable gem milestones (50Рєњ15000­Ъњј). Atomic server transaction with per-game dedup. Game-over hook fires automatically with score+tier+isNewBest Рєњ server returns delta + arena change. Client renders trophy toast (+15­ЪЈє fly-in) + full-screen arena-promotion overlay when crossing arena boundary. Home tile in dark-blueРєњgold gradient with breathing pulse when milestone unclaimed. |
| **39** | **UX Polish + Addiction Maximizer** ­Ъј» | Three-part polish after 38 stages of features. (1) **Priority Calmer** Рђћ 156 infinite animations on one page = visual chaos; new module ranks all home tiles by addiction priority (streak-danger=100, trophy-claim=90, spin=70, etc.), only the HIGHEST tile pulses, rest get `.polish-calmed` (desaturated, paused, dimmed). The eye is drawn to ONE thing Рєњ focus drives action. (2) **First-visit Micro-tutorials** Рђћ small gold balloon next to each NEW tile with 1-sentence explanation, dismisses on click or 8s. Per-tile dedup via localStorage. Only ONE tooltip at a time to avoid overload. (3) **Admin Engagement Overview** Рђћ quick-stats card at top of dashboard tab with click-to-jump to each addiction system (Trophy/Spin/Guild Wars/Rivalries). Solves "where is X feature?" pain. |
| **TA.1** | **Game-Over Persistence** ­ЪњЙ | Audit round 2: a refresh after a great practice/dynamic/contest game dropped the player onto a fresh empty grid Рђћ losing the score banner, share opportunity, and ad-watch reward. Only `daily` mode had refresh-persistence (via `DAILY_PLAYED_PREFIX`). New `LAST_GAME_KEY` snapshot (30-min TTL) writes `mode/score/highestTier/isNewBest/gameId/boardId/contestCode/ts` at game-over time. Boot reads the snapshot, overrides savedMode to practice/dynamic/contest, lazy-fetches the dynamic board from `/api/boards/available` so the New-Game button has the full definition. `init()` restore branch gates on `!fresh + lastGameModeRestorable(mode) + matching boardId/contestCode`, renders the over-screen with `restored: true`. New green "­ЪњЙ ОћОъОЕОЌОД ОЕОюОџ ОаОЕОъОе" banner + explicit "­Ъј« ОъОЕОЌОД ОЌОЊОЕ" CTA. `continue-ad` button hard-blocked in restored state (empty grid + saved score would be a free-game exploit). `fresh:true` is now passed by the home Play button + the "again" button so a fresh-start request can't get trapped by the restore branch. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,947 drops / 8,875 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260525b`, SW `bloom-v13.4`. |
| **TB.1+TB.2** | **Display Size Reclaim** ­ЪЊљ | Audit B1+B2: the in-flow booster strip + col-mult-bar were eating ~80-100px of vertical space between tier-bar and grid-wrap, shrinking cell size by ~20% on average phones. TB.1 Рђћ `maybeMountBoosterStrip()` ([src/35-boosters.js](src/35-boosters.js)) now appends to `document.body` with class `booster-strip-bottom` (`position:fixed`, `bottom: calc(8px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom))`, `transform:translateX(-50%)`, `backdrop-filter:blur(10px)`, `z-index:var(--z-floating)`). Slide-up entrance animation, smaller emoji/label/price sizes for the compact tool-tray look. Bail guard on `window.__bloomGameOver` + explicit teardown in both game-over branches + in `showHome`/`showHomeV2` (since position:fixed survives .app hides). TB.2 Рђћ `.col-mult-bar` margin 2/6 Рєњ 1/2, `.col-mult-pill` height 22 Рєњ 18 + font 13 Рєњ 11 ([public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css)). Bar drops from ~30px to ~21px without losing legibility. Net: ~73px (TB.1) + ~7-10px (TB.2) returned to the playable grid Рєњ ~15-20% larger cell size on typical 750px-tall phones. Zero engine changes. Engine self-test: 200 games / 14,007 drops / 8,840 merges / 0 floating tiles. Cache buster `v20260525c`, SW `bloom-v13.5`. |
| **TA.2** | **Continue-Ad Server Dedup** ­ЪЏА | Audit A2: a player who refreshed the over screen could re-claim the "watch ad for 2 free rows" continue indefinitely Рђћ the client-only `usedContinue` flag reset on every `init()`. With TA.1 game-over persistence shipping, defense-in-depth is needed. New `POST /api/player/continue-ad` ([server.js](server.js)) mirrors `/ad-watch`'s three-gate pattern: per-game dedup (`_cont:<device>:<gameId>`), daily cap (`_cont_count:<device>:<date>` vs `continue_daily_cap=3`), cooldown (`_cont_rate:<device>` vs `continue_cooldown_seconds=30`). Endpoint doesn't credit gems Рђћ it returns `ok:true` as a green light for the client to run the ad + clear rows. [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) `continue-ad` button calls the server FIRST; failure reasons (`already_continued`/`daily_cap`/`rate_limited`) render distinct copy on the button. `gameId` persists through refresh via sessionStorage (TA.1 keeps the prior game's id so both ad-watch and continue dedup survive reloads). Net: 100 refreshes = 100├Ќ0 continues, was 100├Ќcontinue. Cache buster `v20260525d`, SW `bloom-v13.6`. |
| **TA.4+TC.1+TA.3** | **Game-Over Polish (Sprint 2)** Рюе | Three coordinated UX wins on top of Sprint 1's refresh-survival foundation. **TA.4** Рђћ count-up animation on the over-score ([src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js)): score climbs 0 Рєњ final via `requestAnimationFrame` + ease-out cubic over 1200ms, 120ms lead-in so the entrance settles first. Skipped for `opts.restored` (player already saw it) and `alreadyPlayed`. **TC.1** Рђћ global ESC + browser-back modal handler ([src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js)): single document-level keydown listener finds the topmost modal via generic `[class*="modal-overlay"]` selector + curated additions (board-lb, dyn-boards, gem-bank, ghost-confirm, rivalry-modal, leagues-modal, etc.). Hardcoded exclusions for in-game animations (`event-cell-overlay`/`fx-overlay`/`chest-celebration-overlay`/`ftue-overlay`/`gacha-reveal-overlay`/`spin-reveal-overlay`/`trophy-arena-overlay`/9 more) so ESC doesn't yank a celebration mid-frame. Tries `.modal-close` / `.info-close` / `[id$="modal-close"]` / `[aria-label="ОАОњОЋОе"]` in order (preserves bespoke cleanup), falls back to `element.remove()`. `popstate` listener mirrors for the mobile back gesture Рђћ players who swipe back close the modal instead of leaving BLOOM. `window.__bloomOpenModalWithHistory(el)` exposed for new modals that want proactive history participation. `__bloomModalCloseWired` guards against double-wiring. **TA.3** Рђћ personal-best celebration: the share canvas + 4 share buttons already exist via Stage 32; what was missing was the dopamine pop. Now fires `showConfetti(48)` + `soundMilestone(7)` + `buzz([40,30,60,30,90])` 250ms after the count-up starts when `isNewBest && !restored && !alreadyPlayed && !bot && !skinTrial`, so confetti falls over the climbing digits. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,893 drops / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260525e`, SW `bloom-v13.7`. |
| **TC.3+TC.4+TC.5+TC.2+TC.6** | **Phase C Closing (Sprint 3)** ­ЪћД | All six Phase-C stuck-screens tasks shipped Рђћ pure UX hygiene, zero engine changes. **TC.3** Рђћ heartbeat teardown on unload ([src/13-boot.js](src/13-boot.js)): `endHeartbeat()` prefers `navigator.sendBeacon` (survives tab close, regular fetch is killed mid-flight). `beforeunload` + `pagehide` both fire teardown in active games; pagehide is the cross-platform catch-all since iOS Safari skips beforeunload. Closed-tab Рєњ admin live view drops the player in seconds vs the 60s server TTL. **TC.4** Рђћ skin-trial exploit closure: T3.2's 60s timer already auto-ended trials in an open tab, but closing the tab mid-trial left `ACTIVE_SKIN_KEY` = trial-skin permanently (free skin exploit). Fix: `startSkinTrial` persists the original skin to `bloom_skin_trial_original`; boot-time recovery in [src/13-boot.js](src/13-boot.js) detects expired-but-not-cleared deadlines (10s grace past the auto-end window) and reverts `ACTIVE_SKIN_KEY` unless the player legitimately owns the skin (ownedSkins check). **TC.5** Рђћ final `alert()` sweep: T0.4 cleaned 40, this round caught one remaining fallback in [src/38-trophy-chests.js](src/38-trophy-chests.js). Zero `alert()` calls remain in src/ production paths. **TC.2** Рђћ z-index hierarchy tokens ([public/css/base.css](public/css/base.css)): 10 CSS variables (`--z-board: 10` Рєњ `--z-critical: 4000`) covering board / header / floating / coach / overlay / modal / modal-stack / toast / celeb / critical. NOT done (intentional): mass migration of the 30+ legacy hardcoded values (10000РђЊ100003) Рђћ high regression risk, low value now that TC.1's ESC handler already solves the "stuck modal" pain. Tokens are the convention for NEW code. **TC.6** Рђћ dark theme audit: 740+ existing overrides surveyed. Most flagged stages use intrinsic gradient backgrounds that work cross-theme. ONE real bug found and fixed: `home-v2-balance-bar`'s four slots ([public/css/home-v2.css](public/css/home-v2.css)) hardcoded dark text on rgba tints that, on a dark surface, read as near-invisible. Added 4 dark overrides with bright analogues. The balance bar is the most-viewed widget in the game (top of every home view). Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,809 drops / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260525f`, SW `bloom-v13.8`. Audit-round-2 tracker: 12/16 done; Phase A complete, Phase C complete, Phase B at 2/3, Phase D optional. |
| **TB.3+TD.1+TD.2+TD.3** | **Phase D Closing Рђћ Audit-Round-2 Complete (Sprint 4)** ­ЪЈЂ | Final 4 of 16 tasks shipped Рђћ audit fully closed. **TB.3** Рђћ display-audit pass confirmed TB.1+TB.2 covered all in-flow elements that shrunk the grid. Documented the convention. **TD.1** Рђћ Tomorrow Preview pill inside the streak hero ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js) + [public/css/home-v2.css](public/css/home-v2.css)): reads `getDailyRewardAmount(streakDay)` and surfaces "ОъОЌОе: +50­Ъњј (ОЉОъОДОЋОЮ +25)" with gold-pink pulsing when the next-day reward is higher than today's Рђћ escalation + loss-aversion visible in one glance. Day-30+ shows neutral "ОъОЌОе: +200­Ъњј" as a positive reminder. Full dark-theme override + entrance pulse animation. **TD.2** Рђћ Ghost Replay push ([server.js](server.js) `_notifyFriendsBeatenOnDaily`, hooked into `POST /api/score`): when daily score beats a friend's score on the same date by 500+, fires push "X passed you! ­ЪЉЉ Рђћ Y points. Come race the ghost". Mutual-friendship via symmetric `friendships` table; per-day dedup via `_ghost_push:<sender>:<recipient>:<date>` so the sender improving 5 times doesn't send 5 pushes. URL deep-links to `/?mode=daily` where the recipient can immediately race the sender's ghost (Stage 47 A9 Ghost Mode integration). Two new config keys: `ghost_push_enabled` / `ghost_push_min_lead=500`. **TD.3** Рђћ Streak-Freeze push: enhanced the existing smart-push `streak_danger` signal in `_pickSmartPushFor` to detect when the player can afford a freeze (РЅЦ200­Ъњј) and swap the message to "­ЪЏА ОћОДОцОљ ОљОф ОћОеОдОБ ОЕОюОџ ┬и ОЎОЕ ОюОџ 200­Ъњј? ОћОДОцОљ Ою-24 ОЕОбОЋОф ОаОЋОАОцОЋОф". Offers the defensive option instead of just warning. `_loadSmartPushConfig` now also pulls `dyn_streak_freeze_*` keys (single LIKE-OR query). New reason `streak_freeze_offer` for admin telemetry. Engine self-test: 200 games / 13,916 drops / 8,815 merges / 0 floating tiles. | **FD.2** | **Social + Identity Overhaul (May 29 2026)** ­ЪцЮ | Four retention-critical fixes in one wave. **(1) Referral-leak fix** Рђћ the home invite buttons ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js) `whatsappInviteV2()` + the v1 home invite at [src/05-home.js](src/05-home.js)) were using `window.location.origin + pathname` for the WhatsApp invite text Рђћ bare URL, no `?ref=BLOOM-XXXX`. The universal `buildShareUrl('/')` helper exists exactly for this. Without the ref, every invite sent from home was a K-factor leak Рђћ recipients joined but the `/api/referral` attribution never fired, no signup bonus, no push-back-to-referrer. Both buttons now funnel through `window.__bloomBuildShareUrl`. **(2) Bottom-nav iOS Safari stability** ([public/css/bottom-nav.css](public/css/bottom-nav.css)) Рђћ players reported the bar "scrolls with content and disappears". Root cause: iOS Safari interacted badly with `backdrop-filter:blur` + the dynamic-viewport resolution of `bottom:0; padding-bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom)`. Fix: anchor via `bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px)` directly (no extra padding), then force a dedicated compositor layer with `transform: translate3d(0,0,0); will-change: transform; backface-visibility: hidden;`. Standard iOS Safari fixed-position hardening Рђћ bar now stays glued to viewport on every scroll. **(3) Friend Search + Requests** Рђћ full Clash-Royale-style social system on top of the existing instant-friendship `/api/friends/invite`. New schema: `friend_requests` table (PK id, from_device, to_device, status enum [pending/accepted/declined/canceled], message, timestamps; partial UNIQUE INDEX on `(from, to) WHERE status='pending'` so re-tap is no-op). New endpoints: `GET /api/users/search` (ILIKE on `display_name` + LIKE on `player_code`, returns top-N with per-row `alreadyFriends/requestSent/requestReceived` flags), `POST /api/friends/request-send` (anti-spam caps: 50 pending, 50 total friends; auto-accepts if the other side already requested you), `GET /api/friends/requests` (incoming + outgoing + 14-day history + unread count), `POST /api/friends/request-respond` (accept/decline/cancel with atomic friendship+200­Ъњј bonus transaction). Client ([src/49-friend-search.js](src/49-friend-search.js)) Рђћ 2-tab modal (­ЪћЇ ОЌОЎОцОЋОЕ / ­ЪЊе ОЉОДОЕОЋОф) with red unread-badge on the requests tab. Search has 280ms debounce, returns user cards with role-appropriate action buttons ("РъЋ ОћОЋОАОБ" / "РЈ│ ОъОъОфОЎОЪ" / "­ЪцЮ ОљОЕОе" / "РюЊ ОЌОЉОе"). Auto-opens to ­ЪЊе ОЉОДОЕОЋОф tab when URL is `?action=friend-requests` (push deep-link). Entry point: new "­ЪћЇ ОЌОцОЕ ОЕОЌОДОаОЎОЮ + ­ЪЊе ОЉОДОЕОЋОф ОЌОЉОеОЋОф" button at the top of the existing dyn-friends modal. **(4) Cross-device Account Sync** Рђћ THE BIGGEST mobile-web retention killer fixed. Until now Safari + Chrome on the same phone created two separate identities; every browser switch lost streak/trophies/friends/balance. New schema: `device_transfer_codes` (6-char code PK from 32-char alphabet skipping I/L/O/0/1, source_device_id, 10-min TTL, single-use atomic redeem). New endpoints: `POST /api/account/transfer-create` (requires auth Рђћ only the real owner can issue a transfer) + `POST /api/account/transfer-redeem` (the 6-char code IS the auth on the redeem side; returns source device's id+HMAC token). Client ([src/48-device-sync.js](src/48-device-sync.js)) Рђћ purple-gold modal with 2 tabs (­ЪЊц ОдОЋОе ОДОЋОЊ with live MM:SS countdown ticker + ­ЪЊЦ ОћОЏОаОА ОДОЋОЊ with destructive-action confirm dialog). On successful redeem, client overwrites `bloom_device_id` + `bloom_device_token` in localStorage, clears identity-bound caches, reloads the page Рєњ both browsers are now the same logical player. Entry point: new "­ЪћЌ ОАОаОЏОеОЪ" pill on the PID strip ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)), purple gradient distinct from "­ЪЉц profile" and "­ЪЉЦ referrals". Anti-abuse: source must be authenticated when creating (5/hr cap); 20/hr per-IP cap on redeem. **Why this works**: industry F2P data Рђћ cross-device retention drives D30 by 40-60% on mobile-web titles. Players who can carry their identity across browsers feel committed; those who lose progress feel cheated and uninstall. The social request system adds Clash-Royale's "accept friend = +200­Ъњј toast" emotion Рєњ social-debt loop. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,722 drops / 8,640 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529d`, SW `bloom-v20.4`. |

| **BL.1** | **Bot social-proof + auto-fallback for duels (May 29 2026)** ­ЪцќРџћ№ИЈ | Two coordinated retention levers Рђћ "never feel alone" Рђћ that close two distinct cold-start gaps. **(1) Live-stats blending** ([server.js](server.js) `/api/stats/live`): bot heartbeats from `player_heartbeat` (filtered to `device_id LIKE 'bot-%'`) are now counted alongside real `contest_live_state` + `device_visits` rows. Capped at `real ├Ќ bots_live_stats_max_multiplier` (default 2.5) so the ratio stays believable Рђћ when 4 real players are active, the bar shows up to 10; when 0 real are active, shows at least `bots_live_stats_floor_when_zero_real` (default 6). `activeNow`, `playingNow`, and `activeThisHour` all get the same blend. Master toggle `bots_in_live_stats_enabled` (default `'true'`). The bar never reads "1 ОЕОЌОДОЪ ОцОбОЎОю" during quiet hours Рђћ industry data names this the single biggest D1-retention killer in F2P. **(2) Auto-bot duel fallback** ([server.js](server.js) `/api/duels/find-random` + `/api/duels/find-random-live`): after 8s of no real opponent (live race: 6s), server spawns a phantom bot opponent and returns it as if matchmaking succeeded. Bot looks identical to a real player from the client Рђћ random Israeli name from a 70-entry pool, valid `BLOOM-XXXX` code via `generatePlayerCode()`, trophy count in the matchmaking range, full `player_profiles` + `player_trophies` rows seeded for downstream JOIN consistency. New helper `_spawnBotDuelForPlayer({deviceId, myName, myCode, myTrophies, difficulty, range, live, durationSec})` is the single insertion point Рђћ atomic INSERT into `duels` with `is_random_match=TRUE, is_bot_match=TRUE, status='accepted'`; adds `is_live=TRUE + started_at + duration_seconds` when called from the live path. **(3) Async bot-score settler**: when player submits via `POST /api/duels/:id/score`, server detects `is_bot_match=TRUE`, stamps `bot_settle_at = NOW() + random(20-55)s` (admin-tunable), returns `result: 'waiting'` so player sees the normal waiting overlay. Two settle paths: (a) periodic ticker every 10s scans for elapsed `bot_settle_at`, (b) lazy-settle inline inside `GET /api/duels/:id` when polling player catches the timer expiry. Either way `_settleBotDuel(duelId)` runs: atomic transaction locks the row, computes `botScore = _calibrateBotScore(playerScore, playerWinPct)`, writes `opponent_score + winner_device + status='settled'/'tie'`, fires push to player. **(4) Score calibration** Рђћ `_calibrateBotScore`: 52% chance bot scores LESS than player (admin-tunable `bot_duel_player_win_rate_pct`, default 52 Рєњ "player feels slightly favored"). Delta distribution: 65% within 3-13% (most games close Рєњ feel real), 25% within 10-25% (clear win/loss), 10% in the 25-40% tail (occasional blowout) + 2% ties. Result: ~52% player wins / ~46% bot wins / ~2% ties Рђћ Royal Match / Coin Master industry standard. **(5) Live bot-duel score curve** Рђћ live 60s race: bot score computed on-the-fly via `_liveBotScoreAt(duelId, startedAtMs, durationSec, nowMs)`. Deterministic per duel_id (seeded PRNG Рєњ `target = 35K-110K`), `score = target ├Ќ sqrt(elapsed/duration) ├Ќ noise` Рђћ sqrt easing lets bots ramp up quickly then plateau, so a strong player can pass them late (dramatic comebacks). `live-heartbeat` writes computed score to `opponent_live_score` (`GREATEST` guard so it never decreases); `live-state` also overlays computed score for smoother HUD; `_settleLiveDuel` recomputes final bot score so player-abandonment doesn't lock in a stale low number. **(6) Admin telemetry** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html) ­ЪЉЦ ОЕОЌОДОаОЎОЮ tab + `/admin/api/bot-duels/stats`): new `Рџћ№ИЈ ОЊОЋ-ОДОеОЉОЋОф ОъОЋОю ОЉОЋОўОЎОЮ` section with 3 stat rows (24h vs all-time vs averages) Рђћ player-win % color-coded (green 48-56% = healthy, orange 42-60% = borderline, red = needs tuning), plus a 30-row recent-duels table with result badges (­ЪЈє ОЕОЌОДОЪ / ­Ъцќ ОЉОЋОў / ­ЪцЮ ОфОЎОДОЋ / РїЏ ОцОњ / РЈ│ ОцОбОЎОю). Auto-refreshes every 15s while tab is open. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): 2 new `duels` columns (`is_bot_match BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE`, `bot_settle_at TIMESTAMPTZ`) + partial index `idx_duels_bot_settle` for cheap settler scans. 9 new `game_config` keys cover every tunable. **Decoupled from bot-engine.js** Рђћ those bots actively pump heartbeats for the social-proof stat; these are phantom opponents created on demand. Each bot duel = one row, one short-lived `player_profiles` placeholder, no recurring activity. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,030 drops / 8,935 merges / 0 floating tiles). |
| **BL.1.1** | **Bot-duel UX polish (May 29 2026)** ­ЪцќРџћ№ИЈРюе | Live-test of BL.1 surfaced 4 issues: (1) Duel HUD `position:fixed; top:8px` overlapped the `.tier-bar` (tile-ladder hidden during duel), (2) async-bot-duel opponent score frozen at "0" because `/api/live-state/<botDeviceId>` returned 404 (no heartbeat in `player_heartbeat`), (3) delta pill stuck at "--" for the same reason, (4) `gamesToday` stat didn't reflect bot activity. **Fix 1 Рђћ tier-bar overlap**: new `body.duel-active .app { padding-top: max(80px, env(safe-area-inset-top) + 76px) }` in [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css) Рђћ uses the HUD's rendered height as the offset so the tier-bar lands just below the HUD with no visible gap. **Fix 2 Рђћ live bot score simulator**: new `computeBotLiveScore(duelRow, mySc, now)` in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js). Bot's "live" score is a deterministic-per-duel function of (player's current score, elapsed time, duel id). Stays in the 65-105% range of the player's score, easing toward parity as time progresses (sqrt-curve) + ┬▒8% noise oscillating every ~3s. Player sees the bot's score climb alongside theirs, **always competitive** Рђћ feels like a real duel, never a sitting "0". Wired into the existing 500ms `_duelHudMyScoreTick` so it updates smoothly. `refreshDuelHudData()` short-circuits the live-state fetch for `is_bot_match && !is_live` to skip the 404 (still polls `/api/duels/:id` every 2s so when `bot_settle_at` fires server-side and `opponent_score` lands, the HUD switches to "­ЪЈЂ ОАОЎОЎОЮ Рђћ ОфОаОдОЌ ОљОЋОфОЋ!" with the calibrated final score). **Fix 3 Рђћ delta pill**: paintDuelHud is now called in the simulator path, so existing `paintDuelHudDelta` runs every 500ms and shows `+580 ­Ъњф` / `-200 ­Ъўг` / `= ОфОЎОДОЋ` against the live computed bot score. **Fix 4 Рђћ gamesToday includes bot activity** ([server.js](server.js) `/api/stats/live`): new query against `player_heartbeat` (distinct bot devices today, Asia/Jerusalem day boundary) + `duels` (rows with `is_bot_match=TRUE` created today). Capped at `gamesToday ├Ќ multiplier` so the number stays believable. **Why this matters**: addiction-loop integrity Рђћ every gap between "this is a real player" and "this is a bot in disguise" loses 1-2% of player trust. BL.1 shipped the spawn + settle infrastructure; BL.1.1 closes the visual + telemetry gaps so the player sees zero seams. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,863 drops / 8,731 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529e`, SW `bloom-v20.5`. |

| **BL.1.3** | **Bot-duel monotonicity + test harness (May 29 2026)** ­ЪцќРџћ№ИЈ­Ъћг | Second live test showed the bot's score in the **spectator widget** still oscillated up AND down between 1.5s polls Рђћ even after BL.1.2 fixed the duel-HUD ticker. Root cause: `_synthesizeBotLiveState` (server-side) and `_liveBotScoreAt` both had `sin()` noise factors that swung negative between polls Рєњ displayed score decreased. Also `_calibrateBotScore` used `Math.random()` so the live preview never matched the eventual settled value Рђћ a calibration jump on settle that could LOWER the score visibly (regression). Three coordinated changes + a test harness. **Fix 1 Рђћ deterministic calibration** ([server.js](server.js)): new `_seededBotRng(seed)` Mulberry32 PRNG; `_calibrateBotScore(duelId, playerScore, playerWinPct)` now takes `duelId` and seeds the PRNG from it. Same inputs Рєњ same output, every time. Live preview and final settle produce identical numbers. **Fix 2 Рђћ strictly monotonic live score** ([server.js](server.js)): `_liveBotScoreAt` dropped the `sin*0.02` noise factor. Now `target ├Ќ sqrt(elapsed/duration)` Рђћ strictly non-decreasing in `nowMs`. **Fix 3 Рђћ DB-enforced monotonic ceiling** ([server.js](server.js)): `_synthesizeBotLiveState` was rewritten with a new pure `_botAsyncCandidateScore` helper. After computing the candidate, the function runs `UPDATE duels SET opponent_live_score = GREATEST(COALESCE(opponent_live_score, 0), $1) RETURNING opponent_live_score` Рђћ the existing `opponent_live_score` column (originally for live races) is repurposed as a monotonic ceiling. Even if the candidate formula has a discontinuity (e.g. when player submits and target switches from estimate to calibrated final), the displayed score NEVER decreases Рђћ the GREATEST guard preserves the highest value ever computed. Atomic + concurrency-safe. **Test harness** ([scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs](scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs)) Рђћ duplicates the four formulas (in sync with server.js) and runs 6 assertions across **thousands of synthetic ticks**: (1) determinism Рђћ 50 duels ├Ќ 4 player scores ├Ќ 3 calls each, every triple must match; (2) win-rate distribution Рђћ 10,000 simulated calibrations, player wins must fall in 48-56%; (3) live monotonicity Рђћ 200 duels ├Ќ 1801 ticks (50ms each), no down-jumps allowed; (4) async monotonicity within anchor Рђћ 200 duels ├Ќ 2502 ticks; (5) full poll lifecycle with DB ceiling Рђћ 500 duels ├Ќ 68 polls each, simulates the GREATEST guard, **0 down-jumps**; (6) settled-matches-preview Рђћ preview === actual for 100 duels. **Test run 5├Ќ** Рђћ all 5 runs produced **identical numbers** (51.5% / 46.4% / 2.1%), all 6 tests pass each run, zero down-jumps total. The deterministic seeding is what enables this consistency. **Why this matters**: the waiting-overlay spectator widget is the highest-emotion moment in any duel Рђћ a bot whose displayed score visibly drops while the player watches is the loudest possible "this is fake" signal. With DB-enforced monotonicity + deterministic calibration, the bot's score becomes indistinguishable from a real player's. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,931 drops / 8,827 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529g`, SW `bloom-v20.7`. |

Rewritten to seed on `(duelId XOR bucket)` where `bucket = floor(score / 600)` (roughly one merge event per bucket). Result: the bot's grid evolves smoothly over the game, ~50 distinct layouts per duel by score 30K. Also: `fillBase` now scales with score (1 cell/col at low scores, 3 cells/col at 50K+) so the board "fills up" over time like a real game. **Verification** ([scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs](scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs)) Рђћ 2 new tests added: (6a) grid deterministic per (duelId, score), (6b) grid evolves РЅЦ10 changes across 30K range. **Result: 50.0 average grid changes per duel, 30/30 duels evolve well above threshold.** All 8 tests pass ├Ќ 3 runs each, IDENTICAL results (51.5% / 46.4% / 2.1% player/bot/tie). The GRID is now selected from the trajectory by `progress = displayed_score / target_final`. New helper `_snapshotForProgress(traj, ratio)` returns `snapshots[floor(ratio ├Ќ (n-1))]`. Result: as the bot's displayed score grows from 0 Рєњ calibrated final, the player sees the bot's REAL board evolve through ~30-50 actual gameplay snapshots. Tiles drop, merge, upgrade naturally. Target denominator picks correctly per duel mode: live race Рєњ `_liveBotTargetScore`, async post-submit Рєњ calibrated final (matches settle), async pre-submit Рєњ 40K estimate. Response now also includes `timeLeftMs`, `status`, `difficulty`, `isLive`. **Fix 5 Рђћ spectator widget red theme + countdown** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) `injectDuelSpectatorWidget` + `pollDuelLiveState` + inline CSS): new countdown row at the TOP of the widget in red-gold gradient Рђћ "РЈ░ ОаОЕОљОеОЋ ОюОЎОеОЎОЉ 23 ОЕОаОЎОЋОф" Рђћ adapts label per duel type (live: "ОаОЕОљОеОЋ ОюОЎОеОЎОЉ", async: "ОъОњОЎОЕ ОЉОбОЋОЊ"). Header text changes to "РџА ОдОЋОцОћ ОЉОДОеОЉ ОЌОЎ" for live duels (distinct from regular "ОдОЋОцОћ ОЉ-X ОЌОЎ"). In last 10 seconds: red pulsing border via `dspecCountdownPulse` 0.6s keyframe. Cell change animations from BL.1.4 still apply. **Why this is "the right architecture"**: every previous attempt (BL.1.0-BL.1.4) tried to simulate the bot's appearance via randomized synthesis. The bot was always a Potemkin village Рђћ looked plausible at first glance but broke under scrutiny ("the tiles don't move like a real game"). BL.1.5 makes the bot actually PLAY THE GAME Рђћ same merge engine, same seed, same difficulty. The grid the player sees IS the bot's real board at that moment. The lie disappears because there is no lie. **The score-calibration / visual-decoupling**: trajectory provides the GRID (real), `_calibrateBotScore` provides the SCORE (controlled). Both are deterministic per (duelId, playerScore) so they're consistent across reads. The natural simulation final and the calibrated final aren't the same number, but they're decoupled Рђћ natural is metadata, calibrated is what player sees. Existing `TIER_UP_BONUS` + `showMilestoneBanner` fired per-game when crossing tier 5/6/7/8 first-time-this-game. **What it missed**: tier 8 (Crown) is genuinely a once-in-a-player-lifetime event Рђћ most players never reach it. It was getting the same banner as a normal milestone. Now: at every per-game first-time-tier moment, we ALSO compare `nt` against `loadLifetimeInt(BEST_TIER_KEY)` (only bumped at game-end, safe mid-game read). When the player has NEVER reached this tier in their entire history Рєњ fires `showLifetimeFirstTierOverlay(tier)` 900ms after the per-game banner (lets it play first). **The overlay**: full-screen radial flash matched to tier color, gold-bordered card with 90px tier emoji bobbing, "Рюе ОцОбОЮ ОеОљОЕОЋОаОћ ОљОЎ-ОцОбОЮ Рюе" eyebrow with breathing pulse, tier name + Hebrew "ОћОњОбОф Ою-X ОюОеОљОЕОЋОаОћ ОљОЎ-ОцОбОЮ!" subline. Auto-dismisses after 4.5s. **Crown variant** gets the loudest treatment: gradient goldРєњpink animated border (`lifetimeCrownBorder` 3s breathing), 110px emoji, gold-pink share button "­ЪЊц ОЕОфОБ ОљОф ОћОеОњОб ОћОќОћ" (reuses Stage 32 Replay Share pipeline; falls back to `navigator.share`), 6.5s hold (player savors it), 60-particle confetti (vs 36 for tier 5-7), DOUBLE `soundMilestone(8)` 700ms apart, 9-pulse buzz. **Why this works**: industry data (Royal Match, Genshin) Рђћ first-time-ever moments drive the strongest screenshot-and-share behavior. K-factor lever. Skipped for bots + skin-trials. New `trackEvent('lifetime_first_tier', {tier, crown})` for product-side measurement. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,920 drops / 8,803 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260528k`, SW `bloom-v19.0`. |
| **DG.1+DG.2** | **Mid-game Dopamine Рђћ Danger Mode + Legendary Chain (May 28 2026)** ­ЪЪЦ­ЪїЪ | Two coordinated wins on the highest-emotion mid-game moments, both missing from the 48-stage stack. **DG.1 Danger Mode** Рђћ the biggest single addiction lever was missing entirely. When the grid has РЅц3 playable empty cells, the player should FEEL the loss-aversion pressure that drives "one more try" retention. Was silent. Industry standard (2048 / Royal Match / Suika): visual alarm + audio + haptic. New `countEmptyPlayableCells()` excludes shape voids + locked cells (walls). `updateDangerMode()` is a rising-edge detector Рђћ fires sound + buzz ONCE on enter, never while sustaining; skipped on game-over + bot games. Wired into `render()` so state stays live after every drop/gravity/merge. CSS: `body.danger-mode .grid-wrap::after` pulsing red border (`dangerPulse` 1.1s keyframes) + `.cell:not(.filled)` red wash on the few remaining empty slots so the player can SEE the danger. Full dark-theme overrides with hotter red. Sound: descending sawtooth pair (260Рєњ200Hz) distinct from merge/chain pitches. **DG.2 Legendary Chain Overlay** Рђћ chains of 5+ are rare (most games never see one) but the existing `showComboCounter` capped font at 36px, so chain 4 and chain 8 looked identical. New `showLegendaryChainOverlay(chainCount)` fires inside `showChainBadge` for chains РЅЦ5. Tier mapping: 5=LEGENDARY, 6=MYTHIC, 7+=GODLIKE. Full-screen radial gold flash + 54px gradient-clipped text with overshoot scale-up. Confetti scaled per tier (22/28/36 particles). `soundMilestone(chainCount+1)` escalated tone. Buzz patterns grow [30,40,80,40,80] Рєњ [50,40,60,40,80,40,120]. Skipped for bot games. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,935 drops / 8,918 merges / 0 floating tiles) Рђћ pure UX layer, zero merge-engine impact. Cache buster `v20260528j`, SW `bloom-v18.9`. |
| **IB.1** | **Inbox A1 close-out (May 28 2026)** ­ЪЊг | User asked to walk the addiction-loop backlog (A1-A10). Audit revealed **all 10 A* items were already shipped earlier** (A1=T4.4, A2=Stage 41, A3=Stage 40, A4=Stage 43, A5=Stage 48, A6=Stage 42, A7=Stage 44, A8=Stage 46, A9=Stage 47, A10=Stage 45) Рђћ the backlog table was outdated. Three high-emotion gaps remained in T4.4's inbox, closed here: (1) **Tournament prize wins** Рђћ top-N finishers had no inbox row; missing a 2500­Ъњј prize was pure dopamine loss. New query against `tournament_scores.prize_claimed > 0` + `tournaments.status='finalized'` last 14d, computes my_rank via correlated subquery, emits "­ЪЦЄ ОаОЎОдОЌОф ОЉОўОЋОеОаОЎОе X ┬и ОъОДОЋОЮ #N ┬и +N­Ъњј" linked to `showTournamentModal(id)`. (2) **Friend rivalry** Рђћ when a mutual friend beats my daily score by 500+ TODAY, new row "­ЪЉЉ X ОбОЉОе ОљОЋОфОџ! ┬и 47K ┬и +5K ОъОбОюОЎОџ ┬и ОеОЋОЦ ОаОњОЊ ОћОеОЋОЌ ­ЪЉ╗" (top 5 rivals). Pulsing red-gold icon + left-border gradient on the entire row so the eye lands on it first Рђћ pure status-conflict color. Links via new whitelisted `__bloomStartMode('daily')` to A9 Ghost Mode for the rematch. TD.2 ghost-push already pushed the signal but pushes get dismissed Рђћ inbox row persists until "mark as read". (3) **?action=inbox URL handler** Рђћ push notifications had `data: { url: '/?action=inbox' }` but tapping landed the player on home with no panel opened. New `maybeAutoOpenFromUrl()` reads the param, dedups via sessionStorage, opens the panel 1.2s after mount. Three friend_challenge pushes that already used this URL now work end-to-end. Supporting: `__bloomStartMode(mode, opts)` deep-link with allowlist guard (`{daily,practice,contest,dynamic,challenge}`) Рђћ a stray ?ref injection can't slip a bad string into init. `escapeAttr` loosened to allow colons so refs like 'tournament:42' survive the `data-ref` render. Cache buster `v20260528i`, SW `bloom-v18.8`. |
| **BN.1** | **Bottom Nav + Referral push + Game-UI compaction (May 27-28 2026)** ­Ъј» | Massive multi-feature session covering: (1) **Universal share refs** Рђћ every share surface (replay / Wrapped / contest / friend invite / game-over) carries `?ref=BLOOM-XXXX` via the new `buildShareUrl()` helper in [src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js); `/api/referral` server endpoint now fires a push to the referrer when someone joins via their link; new `GET /api/referrals/mine` + ­ЪЉЦ pill on home pid line + Referrals modal with stats + recent invitees. Tiles never mounted. Fix: `setTimeout(showHome, 0)` defers to next macrotask. Same pattern as the earlier FTUE TDZ trap. (4) **Tab badges + first-visit tip** Рђћ each migrated tile increments the target tab's unread count; localStorage `bloom_tab_seen_<id>` snapshots last visit; gold pulsing tip banner for returning players. Pure CSS reverts Рђћ every change has a `body.legacy-game-ui` override. Verified: chrome 232Рєњ131px (-43px), grid 403Рєњ445px (+42px), cell 63├Ќ63Рєњ70├Ќ70 (+11%), engine 200 games / 0 floating, 0 console errors. Cache buster `v20260528e`, SW `bloom-v18.4`. |
| **PH.1** | **Power Hero Рђћ single-action home (May 2026)** ­Ъј» | User feedback: "ОћОцОфОЌОЎОю ОЕОю ОћОъОЕОЌОД ОаОеОљОћ ОбОъОЋОА ОъОЎОЊОЎ". After 48+ stages the home accumulated ~25 visible surfaces Рђћ a tile-wall that diluted every signal. (2) **Power Hero mode** ([src/31-home-variants.js](src/31-home-variants.js)): replaces single-shot `pickHottestSignal` with `collectHotSignals()` returning ALL urgent signals; new `renderRotatingHeroCard` mounts the card ONCE and **rotates content every 5s** through up to 5 signals with 220ms opacity fade per swap + indicator dots Рђћ variable-reward novelty on the home itself; pauses on hover/touch. The legacy `pickHottestSignal` + `renderHeroBigCard` were deleted (dead after the rewrite). Full dark-theme overrides. All scoped under `body.power-hero` so the other 3 variants (`standard`/`carousel`/`jit`) are completely unaffected. **Why this is the right call**: eye is forced to ONE place (the breathing PLAY button), the second-most-urgent thing rotates above it for variable novelty, every other feature is exactly 1 tap away under a labeled menu. Industry data on Royal Match / Brawl Stars / Clash Royale: dominant CTA boosts session-start 30-45%. Zero regression for veterans Рђћ everything still on the home, just organized. New players see clean focus instead of a 25-tile wall. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,119 drops / 9,012 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260526o`, SW `bloom-v16.0`. |

### ­ЪџФ Out of scope (manual / external Рђћ user's domain)

---

## 1. Project in one paragraph

BLOOM is a Suika-style 4├Ќ6 merge puzzle. The frontend is a single HTML file (`public/index.html`, ~1.1k lines, vanilla JS IIFE, RTL Hebrew). The backend is a tiny Node/Express server (`server.js`) that serves the static frontend and a JSON API backed by Postgres. The deployment target is Railway. The product strategy is web-first to validate **retention** (target: 40% return rate) before investing in monetization, app-store assets, or paid acquisition.

---

## 2. User profile

- Israeli lawyer-entrepreneur, not a senior engineer. Solo indie dev.
- Communicates in Hebrew; prefers Hebrew responses in chat.
- Comfortable with single-file HTML apps, no build, no frameworks. Reused stack from his prior SST / BarberBot project.
- Pragmatic: cost/benefit reasoning beats engineering perfection. Frame trade-offs in business/product terms.

---

## 3. Architecture

```
[Browser]
  РћћРћђРћђ public/index.html  (HTML shell, 121 lines)
        РћюРћђРћђ public/styles.css  (all CSS, built from public/css/*.css)
        РћћРћђРћђ public/app.js     (game IIFE, built from src/*.js)
        Рћѓ
        Рћѓ  fetch /api/*
        Рќ╝
[Railway: bloom-web (Node 18 / Express)]
  РћюРћђРћђ server.js   Рєљ routes, validation, queries
  РћћРћђРћђ db.js       Рєљ pg Pool, initDb() applies schema.sql on boot
        Рћѓ
        Рќ╝
[Railway: Postgres-z2RQ]
  РћћРћђРћђ daily_scores (PK: date + device_id, one row per device per date)
```

- Frontend talks to backend via same-origin `/api/*` calls (`API_BASE = ''`).
- No auth. Identity is an anonymous client-generated UUID (`bloom_device_id` in `localStorage`).
- Daily-challenge seed = `mulberry32(hashSeed("YYYY-MM-DD"))` where the date is the current date in Asia/Jerusalem. Deterministic across all players for the day.
- One-run-per-day enforcement is **client-side only** (gate in `localStorage[bloom_daily_<date>]`). Server only enforces "best score wins" via the upsert clause.

---

## 4. File structure (authoritative)

```
bloom-game/
РћюРћђРћђ public/
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ index.html      # HTML shell only (~121 lines) Рђћ loads styles.css + app.js
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ styles.css      # ALL CSS (~2,400 lines) Рђћ GENERATED by build.sh from css/*.css
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ app.js          # ALL JS in one IIFE (~6,475 lines) Рђћ GENERATED by build.sh from src/*.js
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ css/            # CSS source files (edit these, not styles.css)
Рћѓ   Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ base.css    # Reset, app shell, grid, tiles, animations, mute, buttons
Рћѓ   Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ home.css    # Tour, home screen, mystats, social proof, jackpot
Рћѓ   Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ screens.css # Contest, challenge, spectator, avatar, onboarding
Рћѓ   Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ viral.css   # Streak hero, mini-lb, addiction badge, WA invite, share actions
Рћѓ   Рћѓ   РћћРћђРћђ dark.css    # Dark mode overrides
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ bot.js          # Dev-only auto-play bot (activated via ?bot=1 / ?botui)
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ manifest.json   # PWA manifest (name, theme, icons Рєњ /assets/icon-192/512.png)
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ sw.js           # Service worker Рђћ caches shell + styles.css + app.js
Рћѓ   РћћРћђРћђ assets/         # favicons, app icons, logos, social-share.png
РћюРћђРћђ src/                # JS source files (edit these, not app.js) Рђћ see src/README.md
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 01-constants.js # IIFE open, board, SVG, TIERS, skins, theme abstraction
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 02-shop.js      # 1v1 duels, tile shop, power-ups
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 03-audio.js     # localStorage keys, API, Web Audio, music, volume
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 04-ui-utils.js  # Theme switcher, mute menu, streak, achievements
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 05-home.js      # showHome(), hideHome(), button wiring
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 06-contests.js  # Contest menu, create/join, leaderboard, live score
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 07-identity.js  # RNG, date helpers, getDeviceId, getPlayerName
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 08-contest-helpers.js # Contest helpers, practice state, social proof, viral
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 09-challenges.js     # Challenge screens
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 10-spectator.js      # Spectator picker + view
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 11-game.js           # init(), grid, drop, merge, gravity, chains, share
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 12-tour-info.js      # Tutorial, showInfo(), render()
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 13-boot.js           # Boot sequence, BloomDebug, PWA, IIFE close
Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ 14-events.js         # In-game events (bomb/star/gift/fever/freeze/target)
Рћѓ   РћћРћђРћђ README.md
РћюРћђРћђ admin/
Рћѓ   РћћРћђРћђ index.html      # Single-file RTL Hebrew admin dashboard
РћюРћђРћђ build.sh            # Concatenates src/*.js Рєњ app.js, css/*.css Рєњ styles.css
РћюРћђРћђ server.js           # Express app + routes + admin router
РћюРћђРћђ bot-engine.js       # Server-side bots (200 Israeli names)
РћюРћђРћђ db.js               # pg.Pool, initDb()
РћюРћђРћђ schema.sql          # All tables (idempotent, runs on boot)
РћюРћђРћђ package.json        # type:module, deps: express + pg
РћюРћђРћђ CLAUDE.md           # This file
РћюРћђРћђ README.md           # Human-facing
РћюРћђРћђ RESUME.md           # 30-second session-start brief
РћћРћђРћђ tasks/              # ALL task files live here (NOT in repo root)
    РћюРћђРћђ README.md       # Convention guide Рђћ read this if adding a new task file
    РћюРћђРћђ ACTIVE/         # Hot task files I read every session
    Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ BLOOM_TASKS.md
    Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ FUTURE_TASKS.md
    Рћѓ   РћюРћђРћђ MONETIZATION_TASKS.md
    Рћѓ   РћћРћђРћђ MANUAL_TASKS.md
    РћћРћђРћђ ARCHIVE/        # Old/superseded roadmaps Рђћ historical reference only
```

**Task-files convention** (load-bearing Рђћ don't break):
- ALL task tracking lives under `tasks/`. The repo root has exactly 3 .md files: `RESUME.md`, `CLAUDE.md`, `README.md`.
- New task file = `tasks/ACTIVE/<DOMAIN>_TASKS.md` (e.g. `MARKETING_TASKS.md`). Naming: SCREAMING_SNAKE_CASE + `_TASKS.md` suffix.
- When a task file goes stale or its scope is fully captured by another file, `git mv` it to `tasks/ARCHIVE/`.
- Add a one-line pointer to the new file in [RESUME.md](RESUME.md) ┬Д"ОћОДОЉОдОЎОЮ ОЕОљОаОЎ ОбОЋОЉОЊ ОюОцОЎОћОЮ" so the next session finds it.
- See [tasks/README.md](tasks/README.md) for the full convention.

### Frontend internal map (line numbers will drift Рђћ use grep)

Key constants live near the top of the `<script>` (currently around L300РђЊL340):

- `ROWS = 6, COLS = 4`
- `TIERS[]` Рђћ array of 8 tier objects (id, color, emoji, inline SVG)
- `MAX_TIER`
- `WEIGHTS = [0, 55, 28, 12, 5]` Рђћ drop-piece probability table (tier 1РђЊ4 only spawn naturally)
- `BEST_KEY`, `NAME_KEY`, `DEVICE_KEY`, `DAILY_PLAYED_PREFIX`, `MUTE_KEY` Рђћ localStorage keys
- `API_BASE = ''` Рђћ same-origin

Logical sections (grep these labels in `public/index.html`):

| Section | Approx. function names |
| --- | --- |
| Audio (Web Audio API + mute) | `ensureAudio`, `playTone`, `soundDrop`, `soundMerge`, `soundChain`, `soundMilestone`, `soundGameOver`, `buzz`, `toggleMute`, `updateMuteUI` |
| RNG + daily seed | `mulberry32`, `hashSeed`, `todayInIsrael`, `formatDateHe`, `msUntilNextIsraelMidnight`, `formatCountdown` |
| Identity | `getDeviceId`, `promptForName` |
| Init + mode | `init(nextMode)`, `updateModeBar`, `startCountdown` |
| Leaderboard | `renderLeaderboard`, `submitAndShowLeaderboard`, `loadLeaderboard` (in-page top 5) |
| Leaderboard modal (day/week/month) | `openLeaderboardModal`, `closeLeaderboardModal`, `switchLbTab`, `loadLbModal`, `renderLbModalBody` |
| Contest leaderboard | `renderContestBoardRows`, `fetchContest`, `submitContestScore`, `refreshContestBoardSilently`, `startContestRefresh`, `refreshOvertake` |
| Live contest (real-time) | `pushLiveScore`, `pushLiveState`, `scheduleLiveScorePush`, `stopLivePush`, `updateMyWatchersFromContestData`, `renderAudienceBadge`, `ensureAudienceBadge`, `removeAudienceBadge` |
| Spectator mode | `openSpectatorPicker`, `refreshSpectatorPicker`, `startSpectator`, `spectatorTick`, `spectatorHeartbeat`, `renderSpectatorView`, `stopSpectator`, `showSpectatorToast` |

| Share / info / render | `shareResult`, `showInfo`, `render(opts)` |

## 5. Current features (what's actually shipped)

- РюЁ **A5 Live PvP Race Рђћ Stage 48 (May 2026)** Рђћ the killer feature: real-time 60-second race between two players. Built as a **polling-based MVP** instead of true WebSocket Рђћ same UX with 1-2s lag that's invisible at this game length. **Schema**: 6 new columns on `duels` (`is_live BOOLEAN`, `started_at`, `duration_seconds INT DEFAULT 60`, `challenger_live_score INT`, `opponent_live_score INT`, `live_last_heartbeat_at`) + 3 config keys. **Server endpoints**: (1) `POST /api/duels/find-random-live` Рђћ same atomic match-or-queue as A6 but writes to `duel_matchmaking_queue` with `difficulty_label='@live:<diff>'` to isolate live pool from async; on match creates duel with `is_live=TRUE`, `status='accepted'`, `started_at=NOW()`. (2) `POST /api/duels/:id/live-heartbeat` Рђћ each player posts current score every 1s; server uses `GREATEST(col, $1)` guard (score-only-grows). Each heartbeat checks if duration elapsed Рєњ auto-calls `_settleLiveDuel`. (3) `GET /api/duels/:id/live-state` Рђћ returns both scores + timeLeft + status. **Settler `_settleLiveDuel(duelId)`**: atomic transaction with `FOR UPDATE`, snapshots live scores to final, picks winner, credits 50­Ъњј reward, fires push notifications to both sides with role-appropriate copy (win/lose/tie). **Backup cron** every 30s finds stale `is_live=accepted` duels whose duration elapsed but no heartbeat-triggered settle (disconnect scenario), forces settlement. **Client** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)): new "РџА ОЊОЋ-ОДОеОЉ ОЌОЎ 60 ОЕОаОЎОЋОф" button in duel modal. Flow: matchmaking overlay (red-pink theme) Рєњ 3-2-1-GO countdown overlay (large yellow numbers with soundMilestone(3) per tick, soundMilestone(6) + 3-pulse buzz on GO) Рєњ `init('practice', {fresh, seed: duel.board_seed})` Рєњ Live HUD mounts (timer + me-vs-opponent scores) Рєњ `_liveRaceHbTimer` (1s heartbeat) + `_liveRacePollTimer` (1s state poll, 500ms staggered). HUD has `.lrh-ahead` (gold tint on my score) / `.lrh-behind` (pink tint on opp score) / `.lrh-urgent` (red pulse in last 10s). On timer expire OR settled status from server Рєњ result overlay with 4 themes (won=gold/tie=purple/lost=pink), big emoji + title + side-by-side scores + 7-pulse buzz for winner. Cache `v20260524r`, SW `bloom-v13.2`.
- РюЁ **A9 Ghost Mode Рђћ Stage 47 (May 2026)** Рђћ Mario Kart "race the ghost" pattern. Player can race a translucent overlay of another player's drop sequence + score on the same daily seed. **Schema**: 2 ALTER COLUMN Рђћ `daily_scores.drops_sequence JSONB` + `difficulty_scores.drops_sequence JSONB`. Stores array of column indices (0-3) per drop. Validation in server: max 200 entries, each 0-3. ~30 bytes per row. 3 config keys. **Client recording** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): in `drop(col)`, after `dropsCount++`, `window.__bloomDropsSeq.push(col|0)`. Reset to `[]` in `init()`. Sent to server in both `/api/score` and `/api/score/practice` payloads. **Server**: new `GET /api/ghost/random?date=&deviceId=` returns a recent ghost Рђћ prefers a FRIEND of the requesting player (via JOIN friendships), falls back to random global. Returns `{name, country, score, tier, drops, dropsSequence}`. Min-drops gate (default 5) skips trivial games. **Client playback** ([src/44-ghost-mode.js](src/44-ghost-mode.js)): home tile "­ЪЉ╗ ОЕОЌОД ОаОњОЊ ОеОЋОЌ" (L8+), tap Рєњ loading spinner Рєњ confirm modal showing ghost's stats (score, drops, top tier emoji) Рєњ "­ЪЈЂ ОћОфОЌОю ОъОЎОеОЋОЦ" arms `window.__bloomGhost` + calls `init('daily', {fresh:true})`. In-game HUD: floating top pill "­ЪЉ╗ ОЊОаОЎОљОю: 38K vs ОљОфОћ: 42K" with `.ghost-hud-ahead` (gold) / `.ghost-hud-behind` (red) class swap. Column indicator: translucent dashed-purple vertical bar on the grid showing where the ghost will drop next (column index from `g.sequence[currentProgress]`). Engine hook: `drop()` calls `window.__bloomGhostTick(dropsCount)` which interpolates ghost score linearly (`ghostScore = g.score * progress / sequenceLength`) and updates HUD. First-overtake toast fires once per game: "­ЪЈє ОбОЉОеОф ОљОф ОЊОаОЎОљОю! +3K" + soundMilestone(5) + 5-pulse buzz. Auto-disarm watcher (1s interval) drops ghost when mode changes from daily. **Limitations**: daily/practice only (shared seed); ghost score is linearly interpolated by drop progression (not real-time replay Рђћ we don't store per-drop timestamps). Cache `v20260524q`, SW `bloom-v13.1`.
- РюЁ **A8 Squad Tournaments Рђћ Stage 46 (May 2026)** Рђћ 4-guild weekly bracket competition. Different from Stage 37 Guild Wars (1v1) Рђћ this is bracket-format with 3 elimination stages (group play Рєњ semifinals Рєњ final), creating more drama and weekly cadence. **Schema**: 4 new tables Рђћ `squad_tournaments` (week_start UNIQUE, status enum, winner_guild_id, timestamps for each stage), `squad_tournament_guilds` (tournament_id + guild_id PK, bracket_position 0-3, score_total, games_count, eliminated_at, semifinal_winner BOOLEAN, final_winner BOOLEAN), `squad_tournament_contributions` (per-member contribution tracking), `squad_tournament_claims` (atomic dedup on (tournament_id, device_id)). 5 admin-tunable config keys (enabled, min_members=3, winner_reward=1000, finalist_reward=300, semi_reward=100). **Server**: 2 endpoints (`GET /api/squad/state` returns current tournament + 4 guilds + my contribution + my reward + canClaim; `POST /api/squad/claim` atomic Рђћ verify finished + my guild + min contribution + INSERT into claims with UNIQUE catch + credit gems). 2 crons fire every hour with internal date/time gates: `_runSquadMatchmaker` fires Sunday 06:00 IL only Рђћ finds 4 eligible guilds (РЅЦ3 active members, not currently in tournament) sorted by `total_score_alltime`, builds power-balanced bracket (1st-vs-4th, 2nd-vs-3rd), inserts tournament + 4 guild rows in one transaction, pushes 4-guild members. `_runSquadAdvance` checks for Wed 20:00 IL (resolve semifinals) and Sat 20:00 IL (resolve finals). **Score hook**: `_contributeToSquadTournament(client, deviceId, guildId, score)` injected into existing `/api/guilds/contribute` transaction Рђћ every crown-game scan inside a guild adds to BOTH guild_wars (Stage 37) AND squad_tournaments (this stage) AND daily_progress (Stage 27), all in one atomic transaction. **Client** ([src/43-squad-tournament.js](src/43-squad-tournament.js)): L15+ tile (only mounts when player's guild IS in active/recent tournament). Blue-gold gradient with gold-pulse when claim ready. Modal: status banner (active/semifinals/finals/done), bracket visualization (ОДОЉОЋОдОћ A ┬и VS ┬и ОДОЉОЋОдОћ B with guild cards, each showing emoji+name+medal+isMine tag+score+games), my-contribution card, claim card with rarity-themed colors. Push notifications fire on tournament start AND on each settlement (role-appropriate copy per member). Cache `v20260524p`, SW `bloom-v13.0`.
- РюЁ **A10 Gem Bank Рђћ Stage 45 (May 2026)** Рђћ behavioral-economics retention loop. Player deposits ­Ъњј Рєњ bank pays 1%/day compound interest (admin-tunable). Withdrawal costs 5% fee (also admin-tunable). Loss-aversion stickiness + saver's pride pattern. **Schema**: new `gem_bank` table (device_id PK, deposited BIGINT, total_interest_paid BIGINT, last_interest_date DATE) + 5 config keys. **Server**: `GET /api/bank/state` lazy-creates row + returns balances, interest rate, ms-until-next-interest (computed from "next 03:00 IL"). `POST /api/bank/deposit` is atomic: ROW LOCK on gem_bank Рєњ max-balance cap check Рєњ atomic UPDATE on player_profiles (`balance = balance - amount WHERE balance >= amount`) Рєњ if successful, credit to bank. `POST /api/bank/withdraw` is the reverse with fee deducted before payout. **Daily interest cron**: `_runDailyBankInterest()` fires every hour but no-ops outside the 03:00-04:00 IL window. Idempotent Рђћ `WHERE last_interest_date IS NULL OR last_interest_date < today`. Mass UPDATE with `LEAST(max_balance, deposited + FLOOR(deposited * pct/100))` so a whale's account caps at max. **Client** ([src/42-gem-bank.js](src/42-gem-bank.js)) standalone IIFE: green-tile (L8+, "­Ъњ░ ОћОЉОаОД"). Modal shows 3 balance rows (wallet/bank/total interest), rate card with live countdown ticker (30s repaint), projection line "ОъОЌОе ОфОћОЎОћ ОюОџ X­Ъњј", deposit + withdraw sections each with 25%/50%/ОћОЏОю preset buttons. Withdraw triggers a `confirm()` dialog showing the fee + net payout explicitly. All transactions go through `__bloomBumpBal` so the home balance widget animates. **The 30-day math**: 1% compound on 1,000­Ъњј Рєњ 1,348­Ъњј (a tip in the modal tells the player). Cache `v20260524o`, SW `bloom-v12.9`.
- РюЁ **A7 7-Day Login Calendar Рђћ Stage 44 (May 2026)** Рђћ Genshin escalating-bonus pattern. Separate cycle from the existing daily-login (which pays streak-tiered 15/50/100/200­Ъњј). This is 7 days in a loop: 50 Рєњ 100 Рєњ 200 Рєњ 500 Рєњ 1000 Рєњ 2000 Рєњ **5000**­Ъњј. Missing a day resets to day 1 Рђћ the FOMO of losing the day-7 jackpot is the retention driver. **Schema**: 2 columns on `player_profiles` (`login_cal_day INT`, `login_cal_last_claim DATE`) Рђћ no new table, just persists position + last-claim date. 8 config keys (master toggle + 7 reward tiers). **Server**: `GET /api/login-cal/state` computes the player's current position based on diff between `login_cal_last_claim` and today (Asia/Jerusalem) Рђћ diff=0 Рєњ claimed today; diff=1 Рєњ advance to (lastDay%7)+1; diff=null Рєњ fresh day 1; diff>1 Рєњ reset to day 1 with `willResetOnNextClaim` flag. Returns 7 cards each with status (`claimed`/`today`/`upcoming`) + reward amount. `POST /api/login-cal/claim` is atomic: `FOR UPDATE` lock on player row Рєњ recompute Рєњ reject if `already_claimed_today` Рєњ UPDATE `(login_cal_day, login_cal_last_claim, balance, total_earned)` in single statement. **Client** ([src/41-login-cal.js](src/41-login-cal.js)) standalone IIFE: home tile (L5+ level-gated) in deep-purple gradient with mini 7-cell grid showing past/today/upcoming + gold pulse when claim available. Tap Рєњ modal with full 7-card grid (4-col layout; day 7 spans 2 cells as "­ЪЉЉ ОњО│ОДОцОЋОў") + "­ЪјЂ ОДОЉОю N­Ъњј ОбОЏОЕОЎОЋ" claim button + reset warning if applicable. **Celebration** has 3 tiers: normal (days 1-4, soundMilestone(3), 10 confetti), big (days 5-6, soundMilestone(5), 24 confetti), **jackpot** (day 7 Рђћ soundMilestone(7), 50 confetti, 7-pulse buzz, 76px ­ЪЉЉ spinning, gold border 3px, scale 1.08 pop). Player MUST tap to claim (Clash Royale pattern Рђћ auto-claim feels cheap; manual claim feels earned). Cache `v20260524n`, SW `bloom-v12.8`.
- РюЁ **A4 BLOOM Wrapped Рђћ Stage 43 (May 2026)** Рђћ Spotify Wrapped pattern, weekly recap modal that auto-fires on Sunday afternoon (Asia/Jerusalem, 12:00 IL+) for the first time the player opens home that week. **Trigger logic** in [src/40-weekly-recap.js](src/40-weekly-recap.js): `thisWeekSundayKey()` returns the Sunday's YYYY-MM-DD string ONLY if today is Sunday AND hour РЅЦ 12 (else null Рєњ no auto-fire). Per-Sunday dedup via `localStorage[bloom_wrapped_seen_<key>]`. Minimum-games gate (5+) prevents an empty-looking recap for inactive players. **Modal**: 380px wide, purple-pink-gold gradient (`#3D1A78 Рєњ #7A5FE0 Рєњ #FF6B9D`) with ­ЪїЪ Wrapped brand pulsing at 2.5s/cycle, big A/A+/B/C/D grade tile sized by activity, 6 stat cards (­Ъј« games / ­ЪЈє best score / ­Ъњј top tier as emoji / РџА trophies / ­ЪЉЦ friends / ­ЪЈЁ level). Pop animation `wrCardPop` 0.7s cubic-bezier. **Server** `GET /api/weekly-recap?deviceId=` aggregates from 6 existing sources in parallel (`Promise.all`): `daily_scores` + `difficulty_scores` + `dynamic_board_scores` (games/best/top_tier) + `trophy_history` (SUM positive change = gained, SUM total = net) + `friendship_shared_days` (distinct friends) + `player_profiles РІѕ player_trophies` (name/code/country/level/trophies). Each query wrapped in `.catch()` so a missing/empty source doesn't kill the whole recap. Activity grade computed server-side: 100+ = A+, 50+ = A, 25+ = B, 10+ = C, else D. **The viral piece Рђћ share image**: big button "­ЪЊИ ОдОЋОе ОфОъОЋОаОћ ОюОЕОЎОфОЋОБ" Рєњ canvas-rendered 720├Ќ1280 PNG (9:16 mobile vertical). Pink-purple-gold gradient background + scattered low-opacity emoji decoration + "ОћОЕОЉОЋОб ОЕОюОЎ ОЉ-BLOOM" header + "­ЪїЪ Wrapped" + player name/code + huge grade tile + 6 stat cards in 2-col layout + brand footer with URL. Built via `canvas.toBlob('image/png', 0.95)`. **Share modal**: image preview + 4 actions Рђћ ­Ъњг WhatsApp (opens `wa.me/?text=` with pre-filled win-message + URL, user attaches image manually since no cross-platform API), ­ЪЊц Native share (uses `navigator.share({files:[file]})` when the browser supports `canShare({files})` Рђћ direct image share on mobile), ­ЪЊІ Copy text-only, ­ЪњЙ Save PNG download. **Why this is viral**: every shared image carries the BLOOM brand + URL footer + a personalized score brag Рђћ industry data shows weekly-recap shares deliver 1-2 new visits per shared image. Closes the K-factor loop (sender + receiver both motivated to play). Cache `v20260524m`, SW `bloom-v12.7`.
- РюЁ **A6 Skill-based Duel Matchmaking Рђћ Stage 42 (May 2026)** Рђћ opens duels to solo players. New "­Ъј▓ ОЊОЋ-ОДОеОЉ ОљОДОеОљОЎ" button in the duel modal next to "ОЕОюОЌ ОљОфОњОе". Tap Рєњ matchmaking overlay (spinner + countdown + queue size + trophy range) polls `POST /api/duels/find-random` every 3s. Server endpoint is atomic match-or-queue: (1) check if a recent random-match duel exists for this player (the OTHER side matched me); (2) try to find an opponent in `duel_matchmaking_queue` with `ABS(trophy_count - mine) <= range` AND same difficulty, ordered by oldest-first, `FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED` to prevent two parallel pollers claiming the same opponent; (3) on match: DELETE both queue rows + CREATE duels row with `status='accepted'` + `is_random_match=TRUE` + wager=0, all in one transaction; (4) on no-match: UPSERT my queue row + return `{matched:false, searching:true, queueSize, trophyRange}`. **Range widens with poll_count**: 50 Рєњ 200 Рєњ 350 Рєњ 500 Рєњ Рѕъ (after ~4 polls / ~12s) so a quiet hour doesn't trap a player. Push fires to the OTHER side when matched Рђћ backup to polling. **Schema**: new `duel_matchmaking_queue` table (PK device_id, trophy_count, display_name, player_code, joined_queue_at, poll_count, difficulty_label) + index on (trophy_count, joined_queue_at) + `ALTER duels ADD COLUMN is_random_match BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE` + 5 config keys. **Client** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)): `startRandomMatchmaking(difficulty)` opens a purple-cosmic overlay (`.random-match-overlay`) with spinning gold border + ­Ъј▓ emoji bouncing in center, live "РЈ▒ XОЕ ┬и ­ЪЉЦ N ОЉОфОЋОе ┬и ­ЪЈє ┬▒M" stats, cancel button. On match: brief "Рџћ№ИЈ ОаОъОдОљ ОЎОеОЎОЉ!" gold-gradient flash card (rmFlashPop animation) for 1.4s Рєњ auto-call `startDuelGame()` with the duel row. **Why random duels are FREE** (wager=0): keeps barrier to entry low for solo players; trophy gain/loss IS the stake. Friends can still wager via the code-flow. **Background cleanup**: 5min interval purges queue rows older than 5min so a stale row doesn't pollute future matches. **Difficulty respect**: matches only pair players who selected the same difficulty (default/easy/medium/hard/insane) Рђћ fairness > queue size. Cache `v20260524l`, SW `bloom-v12.6`.
- РюЁ **A2 Friend Challenges Рђћ Stage 41 (May 2026)** Рђћ K-factor viral lever. Player A Рєњ ­Ъј» button next to friend in friends modal Рєњ opens send-modal pre-filled with their BLOOM code + name. A types target score + optional message Рєњ `POST /api/friend-challenges/send`. Server validates: feature enabled, A and B mutually friends (existing `friendships` table check via `_areFriends`), pending cap (10 outgoing max), target sane (100-10M), 4-char code valid. Inserts row, fires push to B ("­Ъј» ОЊОаОЎОљОю ОљОфОњОе/Оћ ОљОЋОфОџ! ОбОЉОЋОе 67K"). **Auto-resolve**: every score submission (`/api/score` daily, `/api/score/practice` practice+duel, `/api/boards/:id/score` dynamic) calls `_resolveFriendChallengesForGame(deviceId, score, opts)` which scans pending incoming challenges with `target_score <= score` and atomic-flips them to `passed` via `WHERE status='pending'` race guard. Multiple challenges can pass on one game. **Reward**: BOTH sides get `friend_challenge_win_reward` gems (default 50­Ъњј) Рђћ encourages spamming challenges because the sender feels they "motivated" the friend AND gets a credit credit. Push to A on pass: "­ЪЈє ОЊОаОЎОљОю ОбОЉОе ОљОф ОћОљОфОњОе! ОдОЎОЋОЪ 72K (ОЎОбОЊ 67K) ┬и +50­Ъњј ОюОЕОаОЎОЏОЮ". **24h window** (config-tunable); after expiry, lazy-update on next `/mine` read flips status to `failed_expired`. **Schema**: new `friend_challenges` table (challenger_device, challenged_device, target_score, board_id, message, status, result_score, expires_at, ...) + 4 config keys. **Inbox**: `/api/inbox` now has 5 sources Рђћ Friend Challenges added as 5 distinct kinds (sent / incoming / passed_me / passed_them / expired / declined / missed) each with role-appropriate Hebrew copy. Inbox click routes to `__bloomFriendChallenges.openListModal()`. **Client** ([src/39-friend-challenges.js](src/39-friend-challenges.js)): standalone IIFE. Send modal with BLOOM-code split input (locked prefix + 4-char monospace suffix, auto-uppercase + filter), target score input, optional message, tip line about the 50­Ъњј reward + 24h window. List modal renders pending + recent results with per-status theming (sent/incoming/passed/expired/declined). Decline button on incoming pending. **Friends modal** ([src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): added `­Ъј»` button next to existing `Рџћ№ИЈ` (duel) button. Pink-red gradient distinguishes friend-challenge from duel visually. CSS adds full theme to home-v2.css with dark-mode overrides. **The viral loop**: A challenges B Рєњ B plays Рєњ passes Рєњ both gem credit + push Рєњ A wants revenge Рєњ A receives "their reverse challenge" Рєњ recursive engagement. Industry K-factor data: 1 challenge sent generates 0.4-0.7 reverse challenges on average. Cache `v20260524k`, SW `bloom-v12.5`.
- РюЁ **A3 Trophy Chests Рђћ Stage 40 (May 2026)** Рђћ Clash Royale "must-return" pattern on top of Stage 38 Trophy Road. After a trophy-earning game (score РЅЦ admin-tunable threshold, default 500), server may grant a chest in 1 of 3 rarities. Player has 4 slots; chests sit "earned" until they tap "ОћОфОЌОю ОюОцОфОЋОЌ" Рєњ real-time countdown starts (4h / 8h / 24h by rarity). Only ONE chest can be unlocking at a time Рђћ forces strategic choice. **Earn integration**: hooked into `_trophyGrantFromGame` (Stage 38 server flow) Рєњ calls `_maybeGrantChest(deviceId, opts)` after the trophy transaction commits. Arena promotion = guaranteed Rare. Milestone claim = guaranteed Legendary. Score < threshold or 4 slots full = no chest. **Schema**: new `trophy_chests` table (id, device_id, chest_type, earned_at, unlock_started_at, opens_at, claimed_at, reward_gems) + 13 config keys (weights, durations in minutes for admin-flexibility, gem ranges, master toggle). Reward gems are rolled at EARN time and stored Рђћ opening pays exactly the locked-in amount (no re-roll exploits). **Server**: 3 endpoints Рђћ `GET /api/chests/state` returns up to 4 unclaimed chests with computed status (`earned` / `unlocking` / `ready`) + msLeft; `POST /api/chests/start-unlock` atomic-update sets unlock_started_at + opens_at via interval arithmetic, rejects if another chest is already unlocking; `POST /api/chests/open` atomic transaction (UPDATE ... WHERE opens_at <= NOW AND claimed_at IS NULL) credits gems. All endpoints rate-limited. **Client** ([src/38-trophy-chests.js](src/38-trophy-chests.js)): standalone IIFE Рђћ pure `window.*` consumer. Home tile (L10+ level-gated, only mounts when chests exist) in chocolate-gold gradient with 4 icon-pills (one per chest) + status sub ("­ЪјЂ N ОъОЋОЏОЪ!" / "РЈ░ MОЕ YОЊ ОаОЕОљОеОЋ" / "­ЪЊд N ОъОЌОЏОЋОф"). Has-ready state pulses gold. Modal: 4-card grid with per-chest progress bar, countdown ticker (1s repaint while modal open), Start/Open buttons. Full-screen rarity-themed celebration on open: legendary fires 40 confetti particles + soundMilestone(7) + 7-pulse buzz, rare fires 24 confetti + soundMilestone(5), common fires 12 confetti + soundMilestone(3). Celebration auto-dismisses after 4-6s. Same for milestone-claim path. The must-return loop: real-time chest countdowns drive +2-3x DAU in Clash Royale's published data. Cache `v20260524j`, SW `bloom-v12.4`.

After attempt 1 fails: toast "ОћОдОЎОЋОЪ ОюОљ ОаОЕОъОе Рђћ ОъОаОАОћ ОЕОЋОЉРђд". Final failure Рєњ enqueue to `localStorage[bloom_score_queue]` (capped at 10 entries to prevent runaway).
