Post-build `public/app.js` has zero `alert(` calls. **T0.5 Рђћ server-side date sanity**: `server.js` `POST /api/score` now rejects submissions whose date is more than 1 day away from server's Asia/Jerusalem today (400 `bad_date`). Closes the "device clock is wrong Рєњ daily seed for future/expired day" exploit vector identified in audit ┬ДUX7. Cache buster `v20260524c`, SW `bloom-v11.7`.
- РюЁ **Bot panel Рђћ dynamic-board awareness + leaderboard submit toggle + extended stats (May 2026)** Рђћ the `?bot=1` / `?botui` panel ([public/bot.js](public/bot.js)) had two big gaps after all the May 2026 additions: (1) AI was unaware of dynamic-board features so a frozen / locked / void cell would confuse it, and (2) the bot was permanently sandboxed (`window.__bloomBotActive = true` always) so admin testing of leaderboards still required real games. Three coordinated changes:
  1. **AI awareness of dynamic boards.** New `getBoardContext()` reads `window._activeSpecialBoard` and extracts `multipliers` + `cellsByPos` + `shape_id`. `findLandingRow()` now respects shape voids (from a hardcoded `SHAPE_GEOMETRIES` mirror of the engine's matrices for `heart/diamond/tree/pyramid`) AND locked cells whose `unlocked` flag is still false. `simulateDrop()` was rewritten to thread the context: voids skip BFS/gravity, **frozen** cells block both (matching the engine's anchor semantics Рђћ landing on one sets `landedOnFrozen` and the tile becomes inert, no merges), **gold** cells auto-promote the landed tile by one tier in the sim (with a small +30 heuristic bias toward gold cells), **bonus** cells add their `amount` to the simulated score, and column **multipliers** are applied at the survivor column for every merge (matching the engine's `pointsFor(tier, group, chain, col)` formula). `decideMove()` adds a column-multiplier preference even before merges land (`piece ├Ќ (mult-1) ├Ќ 12`) so big tiers prefer high-multiplier columns, and a -200 penalty for any move that would land on a frozen cell (only chosen when no other column is playable). The AI keeps the existing height/roughness/top-empty penalties from v1.
  2. **LB-submit toggle ("­ЪЊі ОЕОюОЌ ОаОЎОДОЋОЊ ОюОўОЉОюОљОЋОф").** New checkbox in the bot panel, OFF by default. The single behavior switch: `window.__bloomBotActive = !bot.submitToLB`. When unchecked (default), every existing guard in the game code (the ~12 `if (!window.__bloomBotActive)` checks in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js), [src/14-events.js](src/14-events.js), [src/13-boot.js](src/13-boot.js), [src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js)) skips leaderboard submits, achievements, season XP, dynamic-board scores, comeback claims, event gifts, and admin heartbeats Рђћ bot stays fully sandboxed exactly as before. When checked, the bot looks like a real player to every code path: scores flow to `daily_scores`, `dynamic_board_scores`, `tournament_scores`, season-pass XP grants, achievement unlocks, friends shared-day bonus, mystery chest opens Рђћ everything. A pink warning panel + box-shadow on the panel makes the state extremely visible ("Рџа ОаОЎОДОЋОЊ ОћОЉОЋОў ОЎОЎОЕОюОЌ ОюОўОЉОюОљОЋОф ОЉОЕОъОџ"). Toggle is live Рђћ flipping it during play immediately changes the next submit. Defense-in-depth: the daily-score row PK is still `(date, device_id)`, so a player playing daily multiple times with bot ON only gets one row (best-score-wins). The drops anti-cheat heuristic still runs Рђћ a bot drop pattern that's too fast for too high a score still trips `challengeDropsImplausible`.
  3. **Mode selector + extended stats + persistence.** New "Mode" dropdown: `auto` (default Рђћ bot uses whatever screen is open, falls back to practice) / `practice` / `daily` / `dynamic`. When `dynamic` is picked, a second "Board" dropdown appears with the live `/api/boards/available` list (populated via the new `BloomDebug.getAvailableBoards()` + refreshed every 30s) plus a "­Ъј▓ Random" option. Navigation runs at the start of `play()` AND between auto-restarts via `navigateToTargetMode()` calling new BloomDebug extras: `setMode(nextMode)` Рєњ `init(nextMode, { fresh: true })`, `startDynamicBoard(id)` Рєњ applies the board + restarts in dynamic mode, `getMode()` / `getActiveBoard()` for read-only context. **Stats grid** grew from 4 to 6 cards: Games / Best / Average / Top tier (existing) + **­ЪЉЉ Crowns** (count of games where bot reached tier 8 Рђћ the addiction north star, lets admin verify the AI plays well) + **РЈ▒ Playtime** (cumulative mm:ss Рђћ useful for tuning speed presets). When LB-submit is ON, after each game-over the bot fetches `/api/leaderboard/:today` (daily) or `/api/boards/:id/leaderboard?limit=1` (dynamic) to display the player's actual current rank in a dedicated wide stat card ("Last LB rank ┬и ОЎОЋОъОЎ ┬и #14 / 87"). All stats persist to `localStorage[bloom_bot_state_v2]`; settings (speed/mode/board/autorestart/submitToLB) persist to `bloom_bot_state_v2`-paired `bloom_bot_settings_v2` Рђћ closing the tab and reopening the bot resumes exactly where it left off (handy for video recording sessions). Cache buster bumped, BloomDebug API extended.
- РюЁ **Admin-managed skin catalog Рђћ DB-backed shop with add/edit/disable (May 2026)** Рђћ user-reported bug surfaced a much bigger gap: Aurora skin purchase returned `invalid_skin` because the server's hardcoded `SKIN_PRICES` map ([server.js:5523](server.js#L5523)) never got the new id when Aurora shipped. The security pattern from May 2026 phase 1 (server-authoritative skin prices) was load-bearing Рђћ client supplies only the skin id, server picks the price Рђћ but the source of truth was hardcoded, so any new skin needed a code change. Two-part fix: **Phase A** added `aurora: 300` to the hardcoded map (5-minute deploy so existing shoppers could complete the purchase). **Phase B** replaced the whole hardcoded approach with a DB-backed admin system mirroring the dynamic-boards architecture:
  1. **New table `skin_configurations`** in [schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js) (idempotent CREATE + `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` seed of the 7 historical skins so existing players' shop catalog doesn't change). Columns: `skin_id` (immutable string id), `name` (display label with emoji prefix), `price` (­Ъњј cost), `is_enabled` (show in shop at all), `is_sellable` (existing owners keep but new buyers see "ОюОљ ОќОъОЎОЪ ОЏОеОњОб" Рђћ useful for seasonal skins that come and go), `definition` (JSONB: `{tiers: [{bg, fg, svg_key, name, emoji}, ...]}` Рђћ 8 entries one per tier), `special_class` (optional body class trigger like `aurora` Рєњ flips `.skin-aurora-active` for bespoke CSS animations), `sort_order`, timestamps.
  2. **Server endpoints**: `GET /api/skins/available` (public, 60s `_skinsCache` mirroring the existing `_boardCacheByMode` pattern, only enabled rows), admin CRUD under `/<ADMIN>/api/skins` (LEFT JOIN `player_skins` to show owner counts on every list row). New helpers `validateSkinDefinition(def)` (enforces 8 tiers, each with valid `#hex`/`linear-gradient(...)`/`radial-gradient(...)` bg, hex fg, SVG key in the allowlist `circle/leaf/flower/flame/bolt/star/diamond/crown`, name + emoji length caps) and `validateSkinId(raw)` (lowercase alpha-num + underscore, 2-40 chars, must start with letter Рђћ CSS-class-friendly).
  3. **`POST /api/player/buy-skin` rewritten** to query `skin_configurations` first; rejects `skin_disabled` / `not_sellable` with explicit reasons that the client surfaces. Legacy `SKIN_PRICES` hardcoded map kept ONLY as a fallback for the case where the DB seed hasn't run yet (fresh dev env). `POST /api/player/skins/declare` extended to accept any DB-known skin id via a single `WHERE skin_id = ANY($1::text[])` lookup, not just the legacy 7.
  4. **Client integration** in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js): `SKIN_PACKS` switched from `const` to `let` + new `applyServerSkins(serverList)` rebuilds it from the API response on boot, mapping each tier's `svg_key` string back to the matching SVG via the existing `SVG` dict. `syncBodySkinClass()` is now generic Рђћ reads `pack.specialClass` and toggles `.skin-{class}-active` instead of being hardcoded to `aurora`. When the active skin disappears (admin disabled/deleted it), client auto-reverts to `classic` and persists immediately so the next page load doesn't try to revive a dead skin. Shop UI in `showSkinShop()` shows "ОюОљ ОќОъОЎОЪ ОЏОеОњОб" (disabled grey button) when `s.isSellable === false`. The aurora gate in [src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) was replaced with a new `loadServerSkins()` fetch Рђћ the legacy `aurora_skin_enabled` config key is now redundant (admin uses the per-skin `is_enabled` toggle instead, and it works for any future skin).
  5. **Admin UI** in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) under ­Ъј« ОъОЕОЌОД tab: new "­Ъје ОЌОаОЋОф ОАОДОЎОаОЎОЮ" section listing every skin with per-row status pills (РюЊ ОцОбОЎОю / РюЌ ОъОЋОАОфОе / ­Ъњ░ ОюОъОЏОЎОеОћ / ­Ъћњ ОюОљ ОаОъОЏОе / Рюе special_class), 4 action buttons (­ЪџФ ОћОЕОЉОф/ОћОцОбОю toggle / ­Ъћњ ОћОАОе/ОћОЌОќОе ОъОЏОЎОеОћ toggle / Рюј ОбОеОЋОџ / ­ЪЌЉ ОъОЌОД), and a "+ ОАОДОЎОЪ ОЌОЊОЕ" composer. The editor modal is a full form: `skin_id` input (lowercase only, immutable on edit), display name (with emoji prefix), price input, sort_order, special_class (free text), is_enabled + is_sellable checkboxes, and the centerpiece Рђћ 8 tier-editor rows each with `<input type="color">` for bg AND fg, free-text `name`, `emoji` input (4-char cap), and SVG-key dropdown. A "­ЪЊІ ОўОбОЋОЪ ОфОЉОаОЎОф ОДОюОљОАОЎ" button pre-fills the 8 rows from the classic palette so the admin doesn't start from a blank slate. Live 8-tile preview below the editor updates on every input change. Delete with owners present blocks at 409 (`{error: 'has_owners', owner_count}`); admin sees a confirm dialog prompting `?force=1` (destructive Рђћ owners lose the skin Рђћ but documented inline). All mutations write to `admin_actions` audit log + call `invalidateSkinsCache()`. **Limitation**: the per-tier color picker is hex-only; gradient backgrounds (used by Aurora) can be set via direct PATCH or by editing the seed JSON, but not via the picker UI. Documented inline in the modal ("­ЪњА ОюОеОДОб gradient: ОбОеОЎОЏОћ ОЎОЊОаОЎОф ОЕОю Оћ-JSON"). Future enhancement: add a text-input alternative on each row, or build a gradient composer. Cache buster `v20260523f`, SW `bloom-v9.0`.
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 5 Board Shapes (May 2026)** Рђћ completes the original 6-phase BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md spec for shapes. - РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 3F+3G Locked + Teleport (May 2026)** Рђћ completes the 6-cell-type roster from the original BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md spec. `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES = ['gold','bonus','frozen','electric','locked','teleport']`. **­Ъћњ Locked**: blocks both drops and gravity (treated as anchor) until `gameTotalMerges >= unlock_after` (admin-set 1-30), at which point the cell flips `unlocked = true` and renders as regular. Unlock fires `triggerUnlockBurst(r, c)` Рђћ a 30px ­ЪћЊ icon scales up with rotation, a yellow flash radiates outward, and a "ОаОцОфОЌ!" pill floats upward. Per-cell `unlock_after` validated server-side. `isLockedAt(r, c)` returns true only for still-locked cells. drop()'s scan adds `if (isLockedAt(r, col)) continue;` before the empty check. applyGravity treats locked as anchor (writes cursor jumps to `row - 1`). Locked cells are excluded from `reshuffleAllSpecialCells` Рђћ they're the contract between board and player, can't move. **­Ъїђ Teleport**: a tile that lands on a teleport cell is relocated to a random empty non-special non-locked cell. The teleport cell itself stays (the next tile lands there too). Logic in drop() between gold-upgrade and pendingEvent: detect via `isTeleportAt`, pick uniformly random target, `grid[old]=0` + render + 280ms wait + `grid[new]=tile` + render with appearing animation + 200ms wait. `triggerTeleportAnimation` paints a purple ­Ъїђ spiral that scales 0.4Рєњ2.5 with 720┬░ rotation at the source (telSpiralOut), then a matching mirror spiral that scales 2.2Рєњ0.6 with -720┬░ rotation at the destination (telSpiralIn) 220ms later. CSS `.cell.special-locked` paints a 45┬░ diagonal grey-stone stripe pattern + a center ­Ъћњ that shakes ┬▒8┬░ every 4s. `.cell.special-teleport` uses a conic-gradient purple swirl + ­Ъїђ corner spinning at 1.8s/rev. Admin: 2 new paint mode buttons (­Ъћњ ОаОбОЋОю / ­Ъїђ ОўОюОцОЋОеОў), a new "ОаОбОЎОюОћ ОбОЊ: [5] ОъОЎОќОЋОњОЎОЮ" input (1-30) that applies to all locked cells on the board (paired with the existing bonus-amount input), counter splits 6-way ("Рюе N ┬и ­ЪфЎ N ┬и РЮё№ИЈ N ┬и РџА N ┬и ­Ъћњ N ┬и ­Ъїђ N"). Admin guide modal extended from 4-card grid to 6-card grid + 2 new collapsible detail sections (locked + teleport) + 2 new pattern presets (locked-tier-progression with locked row above gold corners, teleport-roulette with bottom teleports feeding top bonus corners). Cache buster `v20260522r`, SW `bloom-v6.8`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,995 drops / 8,828 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 3E Special Cells: Electric (May 2026)** Рђћ fourth special cell type. Extends the merge-group BFS: when the search visits a tile sitting on an electric cell, it queues 8 extra positions (radius-2 orthogonals + diagonals) so the group can absorb same-tier tiles that aren't directly adjacent. Cross-board mega-merges of 5-8 tiles in one drop. `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES = ['gold','bonus','frozen','electric']`. New `isElectricAt(r, c)` mirrors the frozen helper. In [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `findGroup`: after the standard 4-neighbor push, an extra `if (isElectricAt(r, c)) stack.push(...)` adds the 8 radius-2/diagonal neighbors. `visited` keeps the BFS bounded even with multiple electric cells. After each successful merge, the side-effects block scans the group for any electric-cell position; if found, `triggerElectricFlash(group)` fires: every cell in the group gets `.electric-flash` (yellow inset glow + brightness 1.7├Ќ + saturate 1.3├Ќ for 500ms), and from each electric cell, 8 РџА emojis burst outward in cardinal + diagonal directions, each with its own keyframe (`ebFlyN/NE/E/SE/S/SW/W/NW`) translating 280-380% in the corresponding direction over 720ms with scale 0.3Рєњ1.1 and a slight rotation per direction. Cell ring CSS: `.cell.special-electric` with bright yellow inset border (`#F5C400 Рєњ #FFE65A`), 1.4s pulse loop (faster than other types Рђћ "electric" feels live), and a `::after` РџА corner that crackles ┬▒10┬░/+15% scale at 0.9s. Admin adds 4th paint mode "РџА ОЌОЕОъОюОЎ" with `CELL_PAINT_STYLES.electric` (yellow gradient #FFF4B3Рєњ#F5C400) + `PAINT_BORDER.electric = '#7A6100'`. Counter splits 4-way (`Рюе N ┬и ­ЪфЎ N ┬и РЮё№ИЈ N ┬и РџА N`). Tooltip frames electric as "the most spectacular" cell type and recommends 1-2 cells max. Cache buster `v20260522p`, SW `bloom-v6.6`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,081 drops / 8,999 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 3D+++ Board-wide Reshuffle + Mesmerizing Animations (May 2026)** Рђћ extends the per-frozen 'shatter' relocate to ALL special cells with two new admin modes. Now `relocate_mode` allowlist is `['static', 'shatter', 'on_chain', 'on_merge']`. New behaviors: `on_chain` reshuffles every EMPTY special cell (gold / bonus / frozen-without-tile) to random new positions when a chain (РЅЦ2 merges) completes; `on_merge` does the same after every single merge (max chaos). Cells with tiles on them stay anchored (a frozen-with-tile is still a puzzle; a gold/bonus that JUST upgraded shouldn't yank away mid-action). The reshuffle pairs each shuffleable cell with a unique random target via FisherРђЊYates, mutates `_specialCells` + `_specialCellsByPos` via `moveSpecialCellInPlace`, re-renders the board, then plays a STAGGERED 110ms-apart fly animation for each cell. Each flight: a 26px type-matching emoji (Рюе/­ЪфЎ/РЮё№ИЈ) shoots from old Рєњ mid (lifted 40px above to make an arc) Рєњ new while spinning 720┬░ and scale-pulsing 0.6Рєњ1.4Рєњ0.8. Lands with a 4-spark burst at the destination, color-coded per type (gold sparks for Рюе, mint for ­ЪфЎ, ice-blue for РЮё№ИЈ). New CSS keyframes `specialFly`, `spArriveSparkTL/TR/BL/BR` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css). Engine integration in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `drop()`: snapshots `gameTotalMerges` before/after `processChains` to compute `_thisDropMerges`, then triggers `reshuffleAllSpecialCells()` 120ms later if mode matches (the delay lets the chain's settle-render paint first). Admin dropdown expanded to 4 options with detailed Hebrew tooltip framing `on_chain` as "the recommended sweet spot Рђћ rewards skill". The row appears whenever any special cell type exists (not just frozen Рђћ phase 3D++ had a frozen-only gate). Cache buster `v20260522o`, SW `bloom-v6.5`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,962 drops / 8,938 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 3D++ Frozen relocate (May 2026)** Рђћ added admin-controlled "frozen cells relocate after shatter" mode for variable / non-boring frozen behavior. New optional `definition.relocate_mode` field on `special_cells` boards: `'static'` (default Рђћ current behavior) or `'shatter'` (frozen cell jumps to a random empty non-special position after each shatter). Server validation allows the two modes; future expansion to `'roaming'` is straightforward. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,005 drops / 9,000 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 3D+ Frozen polish (May 2026)** Рђћ second pass on frozen cells after user feedback that the "hole below frozen tile" looked like a bug + the only way to clear frozen was a random bomb event (passive, not addictive). Two fixes:
  1. **Shadow indicator** on empty cells below a frozen anchor in the same column. `render()` in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) now walks each column top-down, finds the topmost frozen-with-tile, and adds `.frozen-shadow` to every empty cell below it until a non-empty cell. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): diagonal stripe tint + faint РЮё№ИЈ in the middle with a slow drift Рђћ communicates "intentionally blocked by ice above" instead of looking like a bug.
  2. **Adjacent-merge thaw mechanic** Рђћ turns frozen from "stuck until bomb" into a strategic puzzle. New state `_frozenThawProgress = {}` (per-game, reset in init), `checkFrozenThawAdjacent(mergeRow, mergeCol)` runs after every successful merge in `processChains` and increments any frozen-with-tile cell that's orthogonally adjacent to the merge survivor. After `FROZEN_THAW_THRESHOLD = 3` adjacent merges, `thawFrozenTile(r, c)` shatters: clears the tile, awards `FROZEN_SHATTER_BONUS = 200` points, plays sound+haptic, and fires a `.frozen-shatter-burst` overlay with 4 РЮё№ИЈ ice flakes flying outward + a `+200` blue badge floating up. The cell remains frozen (ready to freeze the next tile that lands). Render shows crack progression as `.frozen-crack-1/2/3` classes on the frozen tile Рђћ visible cracks paint via `::before` linear-gradients, crack-3 shimmers as a "about to shatter!" warning. Admin tooltip updated to explain the new thaw mechanic. Cache buster `v20260522m`, SW `bloom-v6.3`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,985 drops / 8,924 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 3D Special Cells: Frozen (May 2026)** Рђћ first cell type to change the merge AND gravity invariants, not just add a modifier. A tile landing on a frozen cell becomes inert: cannot be part of any merge group, and acts as a gravity anchor (it doesn't fall, and tiles above stack on top of it normally). Below the anchor stays empty (the anchor blocks gravity downward). Only a bomb event (existing) can clear a frozen tile. New `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES = ['gold','bonus','frozen']`. `isFrozenAt(r, c)` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) is the hot-path lookup used by BOTH the BFS and gravity loops. `findGroup` got one new line: `if (isFrozenAt(r, c)) continue;` Рђћ treats frozen tiles as wrong-tier, so they're skipped both as seed and as neighbor. `applyGravity` got a new branch: when it hits a frozen tile during the bottom-up walk, the write cursor snaps to `row - 1` (the next slot above the anchor) so subsequent falling tiles land on top instead of overwriting the anchor. Validated by 3 standalone simulation tests (vanilla / anchor + stack-above / anchor + empty-below-blocked) Рђћ all passed bit-exact. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.cell.special-frozen` ice-blue ring `#6FB7E0 / #B5D4F4` + animated РЮё№ИЈ corner; when `.filled`, a `::before` pseudo-element paints a white-blue frost overlay and the SVG gets `filter: saturate(0.55) brightness(0.85)` so the tile color visibly "ices over". Admin: third paint mode "РЮё№ИЈ ОДОцОЋОљ" added; counter splits 3-way (`Рюе N ┬и ­ЪфЎ N ┬и РЮё№ИЈ N`); tooltip warns 1-3 frozen cells max (more = unwinnable). Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,046 drops / 8,994 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260522l`, SW `bloom-v6.2`.
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 3C Special Cells: Bonus (May 2026)** Рђћ second special cell type after gold. A tile merge whose survivor lands on a bonus cell adds the cell's configured `amount` to the score (admin sets amount per board, 50-10000). The framework now has two coexisting cell types, validating the multi-type paint UI. Server: `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES` grew to `['gold', 'bonus']`; `validateBoardDefinition` enforces `amount` for bonus cells (Number 50..10000, missing/out-of-range rejected). Client constants: `setSpecialCells` in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) preserves the `amount` field when sanitizing Рђћ bad bonus entries silently drop (defensive, never throws). Engine: [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `processChains` checks `getSpecialCellAt(kr, kc)` right after `score += points;` Рђћ if the survivor cell is bonus, adds amount and fires a mint-green "­Ъњј +N" floating badge at the merge spot. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.cell.special-bonus` mirrors the gold visual but in mint (`#4FBD8B` / `#9FE1CB`) so the two are distinguishable at a glance. Admin: paint-mode selector at the top of the cells editor Рђћ two pill buttons (`Рюе ОќОћОЉ` / `­Ъњј ОЉОЋОаОЋОА`), one active at a time, plus a shared `ОАОЏОЋОЮ [500] ­Ъњј` input that applies to every bonus cell on the board. Click a cell Рєњ paints with selected brush. Click same brush again Рєњ clears. Different brush Рєњ replaces (one type per cell). The 4 quick presets (bottom-row / corners / cross / clear) now paint with the currently-selected brush, so making "corners bonus + bottom-row gold" is two preset clicks. The cell counter splits by type: "Рюе 3 ┬и ­Ъњј 4", turns red past 8 (total). Cache buster `v20260522j`, SW `bloom-v6.0`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,828 drops / 8,766 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 3B Special Cells: Gold (May 2026)** Рђћ first cell-level board behavior. Boards can now have a `'special_cells'` type with a `definition.cells = [{row, col, type}]` array. Phase 3B implements one type: `'gold'`. A tile landing on a gold cell upgrades by one tier (capped at MAX_TIER = crown). New constants in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js): `getSpecialCells()` returns the array, `getSpecialCellAt(r, c)` is the O(1) hot-path lookup used by `drop()` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js). The per-mode init logic was refactored: `applyBoardToSession(board)` is a single helper that knows how to apply either `multipliers` or `special_cells` (and future types) Рђћ every per-mode branch (daily / practice / dynamic / duel snapshot) now funnels through it instead of duplicating the type switch. Server-side `validateBoardDefinition` extended with full `special_cells` validation (4├Ќ6 bounds, dedup by position, allowlist of types Рђћ currently just `'gold'`, expand `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES` to add more). Visual: `.cell.special-gold` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) renders a breathing gold ring with a Рюе corner marker, visible even on empty squares so players know where to aim. Admin: the `­Ъћ« ОфОљОЎОЮ ОъОЎОЋОЌОЊОЎОЮ` option in the modal is now enabled Рђћ clicking it reveals a 4├Ќ6 grid editor where each cell is toggleable, plus 4 quick-presets (`bottom-row` / `corners` / `cross` / `clear`) and a live "N ОфОљОЎ ОќОћОЉ" counter that turns red past 6 cells (UX nudge Рђћ too many golds breaks the game). Future cell types (`frozen` / `electric` / `locked` / `teleport` / `bonus`) extend the same framework: add to `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES` on the server, add a branch in the engine handler, add a CSS class. Cache buster `v20260522i`, SW `bloom-v5.9`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,053 drops / 9,031 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 3 per-mode targeting (May 2026)** Рђћ extends phase 2 from pure opt-in to per-mode admin targeting. Admin can now mark each board as applying to one or more game modes: **­Ъј» Dynamic** (opt-in picker, original behavior), **РџА Practice** (free play; score skipped from leaderboard for fairness), **Рџћ№ИЈ Duel** (snapshotted onto the duel row at creation so both players see the same board even if admin changes the active one mid-duel), **­ЪЊЁ Daily** (every player playing today sees the board Рђћ same for everyone, so the daily leaderboard stays fair). Contest + challenge are listed but not wired yet (next round). New `applies_to TEXT[] NOT NULL DEFAULT ARRAY['dynamic']::TEXT[]` column on [schema.sql](schema.sql) (idempotent ALTER Рђћ existing rows get `['dynamic']` automatically). New server helper `getActiveBoardForMode(mode)` + `sanitizeAppliesTo(raw)` + new public endpoint `GET /api/active-board/:mode` with per-mode 60s cache (invalidated on any admin write). Duel creation in [server.js](server.js) `POST /api/duels` now snapshots `board_multipliers` + `board_name` onto the `duels` row at creation time Рђћ pattern mirrors the existing `difficulty_*` snapshot. New admin UI section in the modal "­Ъј» ОЌОю ОбОю ОъОдОЉОЎ ОъОЕОЌОД" with 4 checkboxes; the daily one is wrapped in a pink-tinted warning box and triggers an explicit `confirm()` on save (it's the only mode that touches a shared leaderboard, so the admin must opt-in twice). Client integration: top of `init()` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) clears any stale multiplier, then each mode branch resolves its board (`fetchBoardForMode('daily')` for daily, same for practice, snapshot read for duel, restoration from `window._activeDynamicBoard` for dynamic). [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) `startDuelGame` reads `board_multipliers` from the duel row and applies it before the first render. The fairness guard in 11-game.js leaderboard-submit branch was extended: `practiceFairForLeaderboard = (mode==='practice') && !sessionDifficulty && !window._duelMode && !window._activeSpecialBoard` Рђћ so practice with an active board never pollutes the global default leaderboard. The pill bar in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) lost its `mode === 'dynamic'` gate Рђћ now renders for any mode whenever a multiplier is active. New `showSpecialBoardToast()` in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) fires at every game start when `window._activeSpecialBoard` is set Рђћ gradient pink-orange slide-in pill at the top of the viewport with the board name + multiplier preview, dedup'd per board id so a quick replay doesn't spam, auto-dismisses after 3.2s or on tap. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css). The admin board list now shows per-mode badges (­Ъј» ОЊОЎОаОъОЎ / РџА ОцОеОДОўОЎОА / Рџћ№ИЈ ОЊОЋ-ОДОеОЉ / ­ЪЊЁ ОЊОЎОЎОюОЎ) on every row so the admin sees at a glance where each board kicks in. Cache buster `v20260522g`, SW `bloom-v5.7`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,991 drops / 8,861 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 2 redesigned to opt-in mode (May 2026)** Рђћ initial phase-2 build (commit 825095c) auto-applied any admin-activated board to every player on boot, which polluted the daily / contest / duel / challenge / default-practice experience the user already knew. After user feedback ("ОќОћ ОъОъОЕ ОюОљ ОўОЋОЉ Рђд ОЋОюОљ ОюОцОњОЋОб ОЉОюОЋОЌ ОЕОћОЋОљ ОЏОЉОе ОъОЏОЎОе") the model was flipped to **opt-in**: the admin still creates and schedules boards (`board_configurations` table unchanged), but the **client never auto-applies anything**. Instead, the home screen ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)) shows a dedicated "­Ъј» ОюОЋОЌОЋОф ОЊОЎОаОъОЎОЎОЮ" entry Рђћ but only when at least one board is currently in its schedule window. Tapping it opens a picker modal in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) (new file) that lists every available board as a card with type icon + name + multiplier preview ("­Ъј» ОъОЏОцОЎОюОЎ ОбОъОЋОЊОЋОф ┬и ├Ќ6 ┬и ├Ќ4 ┬и ├Ќ2 ┬и ├Ќ1"). Selecting a board calls `setColumnMultipliers(board.definition.multipliers)` and `init('dynamic', {fresh: true})` Рђћ a new game mode added in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) that is practice-like (random seed, unlimited replays) but **never submits to any leaderboard** (`daily_scores`, `difficulty_scores`, `contest_scores`) Рђћ the existing fair-leaderboard guard already excludes anything that isn't `mode === 'daily'` or a default-difficulty practice. Going home, or starting any other mode, calls `clearDynamicBoardSession()` so the next vanilla game has no leftover multiplier. The pill bar (`.col-mult-bar` in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) + [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css)) is now gated by `mode === 'dynamic'` AND mounted as a sibling between `#tier-bar` and `#grid-wrap` (no longer inside `#grid-wrap`'s flex flow), with `style.width` set in JS to match `gridEl.style.width` so the pills line up exactly with the columns below. Server gets a new `GET /api/boards/available` endpoint returning the full list (the old `/api/active-board` single-row endpoint stays for back-compat). Admin copy updated to "ОюОЋОЌОЋОф ОќОъОЎОаОЎОЮ ОюОЉОЌОЎОеОћ" (available for selection) instead of the old "ОцОбОЎОю ОюОЕОЌОДОаОЎОЮ" (active for all players). Cache buster `v20260522d`, SW `bloom-v5.4`.
- РюЁ **Dynamic Boards Рђћ Phase 1: Column score multipliers (May 2026)** Рђћ first foundation of the Dynamic Boards System (see [BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md](BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md)). Behind the existing `getBoardRows()`/`getBoardCols()` abstractions, new `getColumnMultipliers()` / `setColumnMultipliers(arr)` in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) Рђћ default `null` (no-op). `pointsFor(tier, group, chain, col)` in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) now takes the survivor column and multiplies the base by `mults[col]` when active; when null it returns the vanilla score with zero overhead (validated by `scripts/test_engine.mjs` Рђћ 0 regressions across 200 games / 13,966 drops / 8,905 merges). Single caller in `processChains()` ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) passes `kc` (survivor column, not drop column Рђћ chain reactions can move across columns, and rewarding the *survivor* keeps the strategic choice honest). UI: `.col-mult-bar` pills above the grid show `├Ќ6`/`├Ќ4`/`├Ќ2`/`├Ќ1` with tiered visuals Рђћ gradient-pink + glow for ├Ќ6, gold pulse for ├Ќ4, mint for ├Ќ2, dimmed for ├Ќ1; built in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) using design tokens (`--color-warning`, `--color-success`, `--shadow-glow`). A floating "├ЌN ОбОъОЋОЊОћ!" badge fires next to the merge cell on РЅЦ2├Ќ landings Рђћ gold-to-pink gradient pill, 1.1s lifetime. Activatable today via devtools console: `__bloomDebug.setColumnMultipliers([6,4,2,1]); __bloomDebug.restart();` Рђћ admin UI lands in Phase 2. Cache buster `v20260522a`, SW `bloom-v5.2`.

- РюЁ Tier-ladder "next piece" indicator Рђћ horizontal row of all 8 tier icons with mini merge-points beneath each. Active tier is scaled up with a colored glow ring and its score un-fades to the tile color. After each drop a silent left-to-right sweep cycles through tiers 1-4 (`revealNextTier`) and settles on the chosen piece, teaching the ladder order through repetition.
- РюЁ **Live contest leaderboard** Рђћ while a contest game is in progress, the active player's score updates onto every other contestant's leaderboard view as a pulsing green pill, 1├Ќ/sec via `pushLiveScore`. The pill is shown *in addition to* the accumulated total so the rank ordering reflects the projected end-of-game score.
- РюЁ **Live spectator mode** Рђћ players can watch any other contestant who's currently mid-game. Two entry points: (a) post-game from the game-over modal, (b) **mid-game** from the contest leaderboard screen (`showContestLeaderboard`) Рђћ every row with `liveScore !== null` is `spectatable` (role=button, data-spectate-target/data-spectate-name), wired via a delegated handler on `#clb-board`. A top-level "ОдОцОћ ОЉОъОЕОЌОД ОЌОЎ (N)" button shows when at least one live row is rendered. Mid-game entry calls `saveContestGameState()` then `stopLivePush()`, and on exit (`init('contest')`) resumes from the saved state. Watched grid + score + next-piece refreshes every 1s via `GET /api/contests/:code/live-state/:targetDeviceId`. Watching is cost-aware: the active player only POSTs grid frames (`/live-state`) when the server confirmed they have at least one watcher (`hasWatchers` in `/live-score` response). The spectator's `/watch` heartbeat (every 5s) carries either `lastFinalScore` or Рђћ when paused mid-game Рђћ their *current* in-progress score, so the watched player sees an honest "this watcher reached X" value.
- РюЁ **Audience awareness** Рђћ the active player sees a floating "­ЪЉЂ N" badge over the board with the watcher count. Tap to expand a list of each watcher's name + last-completed-game score. Watcher heartbeat is 5s; TTL on the server is 10s, so closing a tab disappears the watcher from the badge within РЅц15s without any explicit teardown.
- РюЁ **Admin dashboard** at `admin/index.html` Рђћ gated behind `ADMIN_PATH` (URL slug) **and** `ADMIN_PASSWORD` (HTTP Basic Auth). Includes DAU/WAU/MAU/D1 KPIs vs 2026 hybrid-casual benchmarks (40/20/7), 30-day DAU sparkline, 7-day funnel (visited Рєњ played Рєњ completed Рєњ returned-next-day), weekly cohort retention table (D1/D7/D30 per cohort), time-of-day heatmap (7├Ќ24, Asia/Jerusalem), top-scores with z-score outlier flagging (threshold > 3¤Ѓ), contest management (PATCH endsAt/status/name, DELETE), paginated player list with drill-down + cascading delete, "what's happening right now" live view (from `contest_live_state` + `contest_watchers` filtered to 30s), audit log (`admin_actions` table), CSV export with UTF-8 BOM for every table. Reuses existing `cleanContestName`, `isValidDate`, and the rate-limit helper from server.js.
- РюЁ **Visit tracking** Рђћ `/api/ping` upserts `device_visits` rows on each page boot. Lightweight (~1 row/device/day), enables bounce-rate and accurate retention denominators.
- РюЁ **Demo seeder** (`scripts/seed_demo.js`) Рђћ populates 30 players ├Ќ 30 days ├Ќ 5 contests for screenshots/load-testing. Scoped to `device_id LIKE 'demo-%'` and contest codes `DРђдDEMO`. Refuses to run if >1000 non-demo `daily_scores` rows exist unless `--force`. npm scripts: `seed:demo`, `seed:reset`, `seed:clean`.
- РюЁ **UX Polish + Addiction Maximizer Рђћ stage 39 (May 2026)** Рђћ comprehensive polish round after 38 stages. The home had 156 infinite animations on one page = visual chaos that diluted focus. Three coordinated fixes:
  1. **Priority Calmer** ([src/80-polish.js](src/80-polish.js) Рђћ NEW FILE in own IIFE, loads after all other 30s before 99-close). `TILE_PRIORITIES` array ranks every home tile by addiction priority: streak-danger=100 / pet-crying=95 / trophy-milestone=90 / guild-war-reward=88 / league-reward=86 / BP-claim=84 / ach-claim=82 / album-claim=80 / prestige-ready=78 / spin-available=70 / daily-deal=65 / starter-pack=60 / bundle=55 / pet-sad=50 / checklist=40 / guild-war-active=38 / rival-active=35 / passive tiles=4-25. `applyPriorityCalmer()` runs after `applyHomeVariant()` (monkey-patched into the existing window function), finds all matching tiles, picks the highest-priority winner, applies `.polish-spotlight` to it (gold-pink animated halo via `::before` pseudo-element) and `.polish-calmed` to everything else (animation-play-state:paused, filter:saturate(0.75) brightness(0.94), opacity:0.88). Re-runs at 800ms / 2200ms / 3500ms / 5000ms to catch tiles that mount late.
  2. **First-visit Micro-tutorials** Рђћ `TUTORIAL_TEXT` dict maps tile IDs to 1-sentence Hebrew explanations (e.g. spin Рєњ "­ЪјА ОњОюОњОю ОЎОЋОъОЎ ОЌОЎОаОЮ Рђћ ОАОЋОЉОЉ ОцОбОЮ ОЉОЎОЋОЮ ОЋОќОЏОћ ОЉОцОеОА ОъОЕОфОаОћ"). `showMicroTooltip()` mounts a gold gradient balloon next to the tile with auto-positioning (flips below if too close to top, clamps horizontally). Per-tile dedup via `localStorage[bloom_tile_seen_v1]`. **Only ONE tooltip at a time** to avoid overload. Auto-dismisses after 8s or on "ОћОЉОаОфОЎ РюЊ" click. Re-show via `window.__bloomPolish.resetTutorials()`.
  3. **Unified loading spinner** Рђћ `MutationObserver` watches body for new DOM, finds any element with text "РЈ│ ОўОЋОбОЪ..." and replaces with `.polish-spinner` (36px gold-border spinning circle). Consistent loading state across all 14 modals built across stages.
  4. **Admin Engagement Overview** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)) Рђћ new section at TOP of ­ЪЊі ОЊОЕОЉОЋОеОЊ tab with `.engagement-grid` of cards. Each card shows: icon + system name + stat number + status badge (РюЊ ОцОбОЎОю / РЈ░ ОдОеОЎОџ ОўОЎОцОЋОю / РЈИ ОљОЎОЪ ОЕОЌОДОаОЎОЮ) + auto-jump-to-section on click (switches tab + scrolls). Currently 4 systems: Trophy Road / Spin Wheel / Guild Wars / Rivalries Рђћ extensible. Fetches all 4 stats endpoints in parallel via `Promise.all`. Solves "where is X feature in admin?" pain after 38 stages spread the addiction stack across 6 tabs.
  Cache buster `v20260523ad`, SW `bloom-v11.4`.
- РюЁ **Trophy Road Рђћ stage 38 Рђћ Clash Royale pattern (May 2026)** Рђћ the #1 retention mechanism in mobile games. Unlike League/Battle Pass, **trophies can GO DOWN** if you play poorly Рђћ the fear of losing is the strongest dopamine driver. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_trophies` (device_id PK, trophies, trophies_lifetime, highest_trophies, current_arena_id, claimed_milestones JSONB, total_games, total_wins, last_change, last_change_at), `trophy_history` (BIGSERIAL audit log). 11 master config keys + 10 milestone pairs (`trophies_milestone_N_at` + `_gems`). Defaults: win (РЅЦ500 score) = +15­ЪЈє, lose (<100) = Рѕњ8­ЪЈє, crown bonus +40­ЪЈє, personal-best bonus +25­ЪЈє. New-player protection: under 50 trophies = no loss. Safe floor 0. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): 8 visual arenas hardcoded in `TROPHY_ARENAS` (­Ъї▒ sprout/0 Рєњ ­Ъї│ forest/50 Рєњ ­ЪЈў village/200 Рєњ ­ЪЈ░ castle/600 Рєњ ­ЪїІ volcano/1500 Рєњ РЮё№ИЈ ice/3000 Рєњ ­Ъїї galaxy/6000 Рєњ РџА legend/12000). `_calcTrophyChange(opts, cfg)` is the pure calc Рђћ score+tier+isNewBest+currentTrophies Рєњ `{delta, breakdown}`. `_trophyGrantFromGame(deviceId, opts, cfg)` is the atomic transaction Рђћ row-lock, calc, UPDATE state, INSERT history, set per-game dedup key `_trophy:<deviceId>:<gameId>`. 3 endpoints: `GET /api/trophies/state` (returns trophies + arena + nextArena + milestones with claimed/ready flags + stats), `POST /api/trophies/grant-from-game` (rate-limited 200/hr, called from client game-over with score+tier+isNewBest+gameId), `POST /api/trophies/claim-milestone` (atomic claim with row-lock + JSONB array append + balance credit). **Client** ([src/34-trophy-road.js](src/34-trophy-road.js) Рђћ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **dark-blueРєњgold gradient** showing current trophies + arena + next-arena hint, gold-pulsing when milestone unclaimed. **Game-over hook** wired into [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) right after Stage 27 guild-contribute Рђћ `grantTrophiesForGame()` fires fire-and-forget with score+tier+isNewBest+gameId, skipped for bots/skin-trials. **Toasts**: green `+15­ЪЈє` fly-in (up arrow + count) for wins, red `Рѕњ8­ЪЈє` for losses, plays soft tones + scaled buzz. **Arena promotion**: 1.4s after trophy toast, full-screen radial overlay with arena emoji spinning + "ОДОЋОЊОъОф ОюОљОеОаОћ ОЌОЊОЕОћ! ┬и ОљОеОаОф [name]" + 5-pulse buzz + soundMilestone(7). Modal: big arena header with breathing emoji + trophy count + last-change pill (green/red), next-arena progress bar, 3-stat row (highest/games/winrate), 10-milestone list (locked = greyed with "­Ъћњ N­ЪЈє needed", ready = gold-pulsing with "­ЪјЂ ОДОЉОю +N­Ъњј" button, claimed = mint), full arena ladder visualization. Integrated into Stage 35 home variants: 3rd-priority hot card in Carousel + Hero candidate when milestone unclaimed. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `­ЪЈє Trophy Road` section in ­Ъњ░ ОЏОюОЏОюОћ tab Рђћ 4-stat overview (active players, max, avg, total games) + top-30 leaderboard with ­ЪЦЄ­ЪЦѕ­ЪЦЅ medals + win%. New `GET /admin/api/trophies/stats` endpoint. Cache buster `v20260523ac`, SW `bloom-v11.3`.
- РюЁ **Guild Wars Рђћ stage 37 Рђћ clan-vs-clan competition (May 2026)** Рђћ Clash Royale pattern that boosted Supercell's guild retention 3-5x at launch. Auto-matched weekly competition between two guilds. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `guild_wars` (BIGSERIAL + 2 FK to guilds + window + 2 scores + 2 game counts + status + winner_guild_id + finalized_at), `guild_war_contributions` (PK on war+device, per-member score + games count), `guild_war_claims` (PK on war+device, atomic dedup). 6 config keys: enabled / duration_days=7 / min_members_active=3 / winner_reward_per_member=500 / loser_reward_per_member=100 / min_games_to_claim=1. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_runGuildWarMatchmaker()` runs every 6h Рђћ finds eligible guilds (3+ members, no active war), sorts by total_score_alltime, pairs adjacent (power-balanced), inserts war rows with NOW + 7 days. `_maybeContributeToWar(guildId, deviceId, score, client)` is called INSIDE the existing `/api/guilds/contribute` transaction (zero client wiring Рђћ automatic for every guild member's game-over scan-for-crowns hook). Atomic UPDATE both `guild_wars.guild_X_score/games` + UPSERT into `guild_war_contributions`. `_finalizeGuildWar(warId)` is idempotent Рђћ picks winner by score (tie Рєњ no winner), flips status, fires push notifications to all contributing members (best-effort `setImmediate`). `GET /api/guilds/war` returns active war + my contribution + top 10 contributors + unclaimed reward; also lazy-finalizes any expired wars for the player's guild on read. `POST /api/guilds/war/claim` atomic transaction: row-lock contribution Рєњ verify eligibility (min games + winner status) Рєњ INSERT-or-fail claim Рєњ balance credit. Admin: `GET /admin/api/guild-wars` lists 100 most recent (active first), `POST /admin/api/guild-wars/match-now` triggers immediate matchmaker, `POST /admin/api/guild-wars/:id/finalize` force-ends early with audit log. **Client** ([src/33-guild-wars.js](src/33-guild-wars.js) Рђћ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **purple-gradient** (gold when unclaimed reward exists) Рђћ only mounts when in-guild + has active war OR unclaimed reward. Tile shows status text dynamically ("­ЪЉЉ ОъОЋОЉОЎОюОЎОЮ ОЉ-N ОаОДОЋОЊОЋОф" / "­ЪћЦ ОъОљОЌОЋОе ОЉ-N Рђћ ОДОЊОЎОъОћ!" / "Рџћ№ИЈ ОћОъОюОЌОъОћ ОћОЌОюОћ!" / "­ЪЈє ОаОдОЌОЋОЪ!" when claim ready). Modal: optional reward card at top (gold-gradient for winners, silver for losers, with claim button Рєњ atomic claim Рєњ full-screen celebration with 7-pulse buzz + soundMilestone(7) for wins). Active war card: countdown, VS row with both guild emojis + names + scores + game counts, dual-color progress bar (green vs red), my-contribution highlight, top-10 contributors with ­ЪЦЄ­ЪЦѕ­ЪЦЅ medals + names + scores. Tips footer explaining mechanic. - РюЁ **Daily Spin Wheel Рђћ stage 36 Рђћ Coin Master pattern (May 2026)** Рђћ single most addictive daily-return mechanic in F2P puzzles ($1B/year industry). One spin per device per day. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `daily_spin_state` (device_id PK, last_spin_date, current_streak, longest_streak, total_spins, total_gems_won, last_reward JSONB). 4 master config keys + 12 segment definitions (each = 6 keys: label, emoji, type, amount, weight, color). All inside BEGIN/COMMIT. **Client** ([src/32-daily-spin.js](src/32-daily-spin.js) Рђћ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **purple-gold gradient** (Coin Master vibe) with `­ЪјА` icon that auto-tilts every 4s, breathing pulse when canSpin. Click Рєњ modal with: streak card (when streak РЅЦ 1) showing ­ЪћЦ + bonus%, **SVG wheel** (12 colored segments + emoji + label per segment + pointer at top + spinning gold center), spin button. **Animation choreography**: click Рєњ `_spinning = true` Рєњ POST Рєњ on response, calculate target rotation = `-(idx + 0.5) ├Ќ 30┬░ - 5 ├Ќ 360┬░` (5 full turns + decel to target) Рєњ CSS transition with `cubic-bezier(0.17, 0.67, 0.21, 0.99)` over 4.2s Рєњ tick sounds at 300ms intervals during spin Рєњ reveal overlay with reward card. **4-tier reward card**: `small` (<100) / `big` (100-499) / `huge` (500-999) / `jackpot` (5000+). Jackpot card has continuous gold-glow animation + 32-particle confetti burst + 7-pulse buzz + soundMilestone(7). Each tier gets scaled confetti count + scaled buzz pattern. Streak bonus rendered as red-orange "­ЪћЦ +N%" pill. **Integrated into Stage 35 home variants**: top-priority card in Carousel + #1 candidate signal in Hero (when canSpin). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): `­ЪјА ОњОюОњОю ОЎОЋОъОЎ / Spin Wheel` section in ­Ъњ░ ОЏОюОЏОюОћ tab with 4-stat overview (total spins / 7-day active / total gems / longest streak). 12 segment definitions editable via the generic "ОЏОю ОћОћОњОЊОеОЋОф" config table. - РюЁ **Home Variants A/B Рђћ stage 35 Рђћ 4 home layouts pickable from admin (May 2026)** Рђћ solves the home-screen overload problem (the v2 home grew to 14+ tiles after stages 17-34, classic mobile cognitive-load territory). Admin picks ONE layout globally via `game_config.home_variant`. **Architecture**: pure decorator pattern in [src/31-home-variants.js](src/31-home-variants.js) (NEW FILE in own IIFE) Рђћ `applyHomeVariant()` is called at the end of `showHomeV2()` after a 3.4s delay (waits for all `maybeShow*Tile` deferred mounts to settle), then re-arranges DOM based on variant. Every tile's own logic stays untouched Рђћ variants only hide / move / wrap. **4 variants**: (1) ­ЪЊ║ **standard** Рђћ no-op, current v2 behavior; (2) ­Ъја **carousel** Рђћ adds a horizontally-scrolling "­ЪћЦ ОЌОЮ ОбОЏОЕОЎОЋ" row at the top with 3-6 cards derived from active tiles (Battle Pass claim ready / league reward / pet crying / daily deal / etc.), each card clicks through to the underlying tile via a stable selector Рєњ `el.click()` map. `.hvar-carousel-card.hot` has a 2s pulse animation for time-critical cards; (3) ­Ъј» **hero** Рђћ replaces the hero with a MASSIVE single-action card (60% viewport) showing the highest-emotion signal RIGHT NOW (priority: league reward Рєњ BP claim Рєњ sad pet Рєњ daily deal Рєњ bundle Рєњ boards Рєњ rival), with a giant black "­ЪјЂ ОюОљОАОЋОБ" CTA that re-fires the underlying tile's click. All other secondary tiles collapse into a `­ЪЊѓ ОбОЋОЊ N ОцОЎОдО│ОеОЎОЮ` expander above the bottom links. Four hero theme classes: `hero-reward` (gold), `hero-urgent` (red, pulses), `hero-hot` (pink), `hero-neutral` (default orange); (4) ­ЪјЊ **jit** Рђћ Just-In-Time progressive disclosure. New players see only base CTA + pet. Tiles unlock in 5 waves based on `loadGamesPlayed()` against admin-configurable thresholds (`home_jit_unlock_games`, default `3,7,13,26`). When a tile is shown for the FIRST time, it gets a `­ЪјЅ ОЌОЊОЕ!` floating badge + `hvarJitUnlock` 1.4s scale-pop animation + `soundMilestone(4)` + buzz + scrollIntoView (staggered 1.4s apart). Per-tile first-show dedup via `localStorage[bloom_jit_seen_v1]`. Bottom-of-home teaser banner "ОбОЋОЊ **N ОъОЕОЌОДОЎОЮ** ОюОцОфОЎОЌОф..." with next-wave-content preview labels (e.g. wave 4 = "Рџћ№ИЈ ОюОЎОњОћ / ОЎОеОЎОЉОЋОф / ОћОЎОЕОњОЎОЮ") Рђћ the prospective-FOMO punch. **Server** ([schema.sql](schema.sql)): 2 new config keys (`home_variant` default `'standard'`, `home_jit_unlock_games` default `'3,7,13,26'`). No new endpoints Рђћ uses existing `/api/config` public endpoint (returns flat dict `{key: value}` so client reads `gameConfig.home_variant` directly). Rich Hebrew tooltips on every variant explaining trade-offs + addiction rationale. **CSS** ([public/css/home-v2.css](public/css/home-v2.css)) appended ~150 lines covering all 3 non-standard variants with full dark-theme overrides. - РюЁ **Rivalry System Рђћ stage 33 Рђћ auto-paired 24h personal competition (May 2026)** Рђћ the Clash Royale pattern. - РюЁ **Guilds / Clans Рђћ stage 27 Рђћ peer-pressure retention (May 2026)** Рђћ the biggest retention mechanic in modern mobile games. Industry data: +35% D30 retention, 3.4├Ќ sessions/day vs solo players. **v1 scope** intentionally tight: create/join/leave + daily collective goal + per-member reward claim + leaderboard. **Skipped to v2**: real-time chat, clan-vs-clan wars, league tiers. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): 4 tables Рђћ `guilds` (id, code 6-char UNIQUE, name, emoji, creator, member_count, total_score_alltime, max_members), `guild_members` (PK on guild+device, role, joined_at, score+crowns contrib counters), `guild_daily_progress` (PK on guild+date, goal_target/progress, is_complete flag), `guild_member_claims` (PK on guild+device+date for atomic dedup). 5 config keys: enabled / create_cost=500­Ъњј / max_members=30 / daily_goal=30 crowns / reward_per_member=200­Ъњј. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): 7 endpoints. `POST /guilds/create`: atomic gem-deduct + insert guild + insert creator as leader. `POST /guilds/join`: anti-cheat checks (already in guild, guild full) + atomic insert + member_count bump. `POST /guilds/leave`: deletes member; if last out Рєњ deletes guild; if leader left Рєњ promotes oldest member. `GET /guilds/mine`: returns guild + members (sorted by contribution) + today's progress + my claim status. `POST /guilds/contribute`: atomic Рђћ bumps member counters + daily progress + checks if goal just completed (returns `justCompleted=true`). `POST /guilds/claim-daily`: server-side eligibility re-check + atomic UNIQUE-guarded claim + balance credit. `GET /guilds/leaderboard`: top-N by all-time total score. - РюЁ **Smart Notifications Рђћ stage 31 Рђћ auto-personalized push scheduler (May 2026)** Рђћ server-side scheduler that scans subscribed devices every 30 min, picks the highest-emotional signal per device, sends ONE personalized push. Differs from Stage 10 (admin broadcast): this is fully automatic + per-device. Both still work. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_push_state` (device_id PK, last_sent_at, last_send_reason, total_sent, last_scan_at). 6 config keys for cooldown/scan-interval/allowed-hours/batch-size. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_pickSmartPushFor(deviceId, cfg)` runs 8 parallel queries (each wrapped in catch to tolerate missing tables) and computes the highest-priority signal: **(1) Pet crying ­Ъўб** (>48h since visit Рђћ guilt mechanic, highest emotion); **(2) Tournament ending ­ЪЈє** (within 3h); **(3) Friend played today, you didn't ­ЪЉЦ** (FOMO + social); **(4) Streak danger ­ЪћЦ** (last play was yesterday); **(5) BP unclaimed ­Ъјќ** (РЅЦ5 rewards waiting); **(6) Comeback ­ЪЉІ** (3-30 days away); **(7) Daily Special ­ЪїЪ** (after 14:00 if not played today). All messages personalized with player name + specifics. `_runSmartPushScan()` is the scheduler loop Рђћ runs every `smart_push_scan_minutes` (30 default) ONLY during 9:00-22:00 Asia/Jerusalem hours. Per-device cooldown 12h. Marks `last_scan_at` even when no push sent so we spread load. `_startSmartPushScheduler()` fires after 60s boot delay. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): new `­Ъцќ ОћОфОеОљОЋОф ОЌОЏОъОЋОф ОљОЋОўОЋОъОўОЎОЋОф` section with 6 config keys + live stats (subscribers, sent in 24h/7d, total ever, reason breakdown by category) + "­Ъћё ОАОеОЋОД ОбОЏОЕОЎОЋ" manual trigger + recent-30-sends table with emoji-coded reasons. 6 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. - РюЁ **Lifetime Progression Рђћ stage 30 Рђћ Call of Duty Prestige (May 2026)** Рђћ the longest meta-arc in the game. NEVER resets between seasons. - РюЁ **Achievement-driven Cross-Leaderboard Рђћ stage 16 Рђћ new competitive axis (May 2026)** Рђћ global ranking by NUMBER of achievements unlocked (not score). Rewards completionists / breadth-players over single-board grinders. Until this stage, achievements lived only in `localStorage[bloom_dyn_achievements]` Рђћ Stage 16 mirrors them server-side. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_achievements` table with `BIGSERIAL id`, `(device_id, achievement_key)` UNIQUE INDEX (handles dedup), recent-unlock and per-device indexes. Achievement keys are opaque strings Рђћ client uses `cross:pioneer5`, `board:42:crown`, etc. 2 config keys: `ach_leaderboard_enabled` + `ach_leaderboard_show_on_home`. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `POST /api/achievements/unlock` (idempotent via ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING, validates key against `/^[a-z0-9_:-]+$/`). `POST /api/achievements/sync` for bulk-backfill from localStorage (capped at 500 keys per call, 10/hr rate limit). `GET /api/achievements/leaderboard?limit=50` returns top-N players with LEFT JOINs to `player_profiles` for name/country/player_code (fallback to most-recent `daily_scores` name). Includes "me" row + my-rank computation via `COUNT(*) WHERE count > my_count + 1`. `GET /api/achievements/me` for lightweight count + rank lookup. **Client** ([src/24-ach-leaderboard.js](src/24-ach-leaderboard.js) Рђћ NEW FILE in own IIFE): on boot, reads localStorage state and POSTs bulk sync (one-time per session). `grantPerBoard` + `grantCross` in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) now also fire `serverUnlockAchievement` (fire-and-forget) so new unlocks are mirrored immediately. **Home tile**: gold-yellow `.ach-lb-home-tile` mounts only for players with 3+ achievements Рђћ shows "­ЪЈЁ ОюОЋОЌ ОъОЋОЉОЎОюОЎОЮ Рђћ ОћОЎОЕОњОЎОЮ #14 / ОцОфОЌОф 17 ОћОЎОЕОњОЎОЮ". **Modal**: gold-themed with ­ЪЈЁ icon, my-rank pill at top (when I'm outside top 50), full ranked list with podium colors (­ЪЦЄ/­ЪЦѕ/­ЪЦЅ), country flags, "you" highlight. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `­ЪЈЁ ОюОЋОЌ ОъОЋОЉОЎОюОЎОЮ Рђћ ОћОЎОЕОњОЎОЮ` section with toggles + top-20 player list (read-only) + refresh button. 2 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. Cache buster `v20260523r`, SW `bloom-v10.2`.

Live countdown (1s tick), explicit scarcity ribbon, content rows, big "­ЪЏњ ОДОаОћ ОбОЏОЕОЎОЋ ┬и 600­Ъњј" button. **Welcome overlay** on purchase: gold celebration card with contents recap. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `­ЪјЂ ОЌОЉОЎОюОЋОф ОЌОњ` section + bundles list with status badges (­ЪЪб active / РЈ│ upcoming / РїЏ ended / РЈИ disabled) + theme-color left border per row + total purchases/revenue stats. **3 one-click presets**: ­ЪЋј ОЌОаОЋОЏОћ / ­ЪњЋ ОЋОюОаОўОЎОЎОЪ / ­ЪћЦ Black Friday Рђћ each pre-fills the editor with appropriate emoji/color/decoration/price/contents/dates. - РюЁ **Lives / Energy Рђћ stage 19 Рђћ scarcity-driven engagement (May 2026)** Рђћ Candy Crush pattern, **DEFAULT-OFF** (admin opt-in via `lives_enabled='true'`). Limited lives that regen over time + refill via ad/­Ъњј/wait. **Scope**: applies ONLY to dynamic boards. Daily/practice/contests/duels/challenges remain unlimited Рђћ intentional to protect existing UX. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_lives_state` (current_lives, max_lives, last_regen_at + 3 stat counters). 6 config keys: `lives_enabled` (default 'false'), `lives_max` (5), `lives_regen_minutes` (30), `lives_refill_price_gems` (50), `lives_ad_refill_count` (1), `lives_per_game_dynamic` (1). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_computeLivesNow(deviceId, cfg)` is the lazy-regen calculator Рђћ reads current state, applies floor((now - last_regen) / regen_minutes) regen ticks, advances last_regen_at by the consumed ticks, returns clean state with `msUntilNextRegen`. 4 public endpoints: `GET /lives/state`, `POST /lives/consume` (atomic decrement with current_lives >= n guard), `POST /lives/refill-gems` (atomic deduct + reset to max + last_regen_at=NOW), `POST /lives/refill-ad` (per-gameId dedup via game_config key, +N lives). All with rate-limiting. When `lives_enabled='false'`, all endpoints return `{enabled:false, currentLives:999}` so client gates are no-ops. **Client** ([src/20-lives.js](src/20-lives.js) Рђћ NEW FILE in own IIFE): `maybeShowLivesWidget()` mounts a pink-themed hearts widget at the top of home (red breathing if 0 lives). Widget shows: РЮц№ИЈРЮц№ИЈ­ЪцЇ­ЪцЇ­ЪцЇ hearts, count "2 / 5 ОЌОЎОЎОЮ", regen countdown ticker "РЈ░ 14ОЊ 22ОЕ ОюОЌОЎОЎОЮ ОћОЉОљОЎОЮ". Click Рєњ out-of-lives modal with **3 refill paths**: ­ЪЊ║ ad (mint), ­Ъњј gems (gold), РЈ░ wait (close). All disabled when full. `ensureLifeForDynamicGame()` is the gate Рђћ called from `startDynamicBoard`. Resolves true if life consumed or system disabled, false if no lives Рєњ shows modal. Live ticker decrements client-side every 1s for smooth countdown, re-fetches authoritative state when timer hits 0. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `РЮц№ИЈ ОЌОЎОЎОЮ / Energy` section with **prominent Рџа RISKY warning banner** at the top + red ribbon next to the section title. 6 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with explicit "A/B test if you enable" warnings. Cache buster `v20260523n`, SW `bloom-v9.8`.

Pity logic forces legendary+ when counter hits threshold. `_gachaGrantReward` handles all 5 reward types: gems credit, skin insert (with **duplicate detection Рєњ auto-convert to gems at 50% of skin price**), BP tier XP boost (advances N tiers in Season Pass), chest/freeze converted to gem-equivalent for v1. `_doGachaPull(deviceId, multiplier, isFree)` is the atomic transaction: deduct price Рєњ check free-pull dedup Рєњ resolve N pulls Рєњ grant N rewards Рєњ log history Рєњ update state. All in one BEGIN/COMMIT. 3 public endpoints (state, pull, history) + 4 admin CRUD endpoints (placed correctly inside the `if (ADMIN_PATH && ADMIN_PASSWORD)` block Рђћ fixed the bug from stage 21). **Client** ([src/19-skin-gacha.js](src/19-skin-gacha.js) Рђћ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home banner purple-cosmic gradient distinct from gold (BP/Starter) and red (Daily Deals). - РюЁ **Daily Deals Рђћ stage 21 Рђћ rotating daily offer (May 2026)** Рђћ one deal rotates daily (Asia/Jerusalem) from an admin-managed pool. Anchoring psychology ("ОЌОАОЏОф 60%!") + 24h countdown + one-purchase-per-day-per-deal. **Daily-return hook** Рђћ players open the app each morning to see "what's on sale today". **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `daily_deals` table (id, slug, name, description, emoji, price_gems, original_value for strikethrough, contents JSONB, category, is_enabled, sort_order) seeded with **7 starter deals** Рђћ `gem_starter` (50­ЪњјРєњ200­Ъњј), `gem_bundle` (500­ЪњјРєњ1200­Ъњј), `skin_deal` (200­ЪњјРєњfire skin), `bp_boost` (300­ЪњјРєњ1 BP tier), `chest_x3` (150­ЪњјРєњ3 chests), `freeze_x3` (300­ЪњјРєњ3 streak freezes), `mega_bundle` (800­ЪњјРєњ1000­Ъњј+space skin+1 BP tier). `daily_deal_purchases` table with PK `(device_id, deal_id, purchase_date)` for per-day-per-deal dedup. 4 master config keys. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_dailyDealHash` FNV-1a hash of today's date Рєњ index into enabled deals. `_pickTodaysDeal()` returns the chosen deal + date, honoring `daily_deals_override_id` admin override. `_msUntilNextIsraelMidnight()` for accurate countdown. `GET /api/daily-deals/today?deviceId` returns `{ ok, enabled, date, expiresAt, msLeft, deal: {...with discountPct calculated}, purchased }`. `POST /api/daily-deals/buy` is the atomic transaction: re-verifies dealId IS today's deal (anti-cheat Рђћ can't buy yesterday's/tomorrow's), checks not-already-purchased, deducts price with balance guard, grants gems/skin/BP-tiers/etc atomically, inserts purchase record. Returns `{ok, granted: {...}, newBalance}`. 4 admin CRUD endpoints for managing the pool. **Client** ([src/18-daily-deals.js](src/18-daily-deals.js) Рђћ NEW FILE in its own IIFE): `maybeShowDailyDealBanner()` fetched on home mount, mounts a red-orange `.daily-deal-home-banner` AFTER the starter-pack banner (so starter takes priority). Live countdown in modal too Рђћ auto-disables buy button when expired. Click РюЈ№ИЈ opens a full modal editor with all fields: slug (locked on edit), emoji, name, description, prices, contents grid (5 input fields for gems/skin_id/bp_tiers/chest_count/streak_freezes), category, sort_order, is_enabled toggle. Cache buster `v20260523l`, SW `bloom-v9.6`.
- РюЁ **Starter Pack Рђћ stage 20 Рђћ first-purchase funnel (May 2026)** Рђћ the single highest-conversion offer in F2P puzzle games (50-90% buy-through in industry data). Fires ONCE after a player crosses a score threshold (default 5K). 7-day countdown + one-time-only = strong loss-aversion. Pays out 500­Ъњј Рєњ 1500­Ъњј + a skin + 3 Battle Pass tier boost (~5├Ќ ROI). **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): new `starter_pack_state` table Рђћ PK on `device_id`, tracks `eligible_at` + `expires_at` + `purchased_at` + `dismissed_count` + `pack_contents` snapshot at purchase. 9 admin config keys (`enabled`, `name`, `price_gems`, `price_usd`, `trigger_score`, `expires_hours`, `reward_gems`, `reward_skin_id`, `reward_bp_tiers`). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/player/starter-pack/status?deviceId&score` Рђћ first checks if the row exists (creates on first call), if `eligible_at` is null AND `score >= trigger_score` stamps `eligible_at = NOW()` + `expires_at = NOW() + N hours`. Returns `{available, expiresAt, priceGems, rewardGems, rewardBpTiers, rewardSkinId, name, dismissedCount}`. Short-circuits `{purchased: true}` if already bought. `POST /api/player/starter-pack/buy` is the atomic transaction Рђћ server re-verifies eligibility (not trusting client), deducts price from balance with balance-guarded UPDATE, credits reward_gems, INSERTs the skin (idempotent), computes XP boost to push the player up `reward_bp_tiers` tiers in Battle Pass (reads tier thresholds, calculates the gap to `current_tier + N`, upserts the boost), stamps `purchased_at` + snapshots `pack_contents`. All in one transaction Рђћ any failure rolls back. Returns `{ok, newBalance, ...rewards}`. `POST /dismiss` increments a counter for telemetry (player keeps closing the banner Рђћ admin can see dismiss rate). Rate-limited: status no limit, buy 5/hr, dismiss 30/hr. **Client** ([src/17-starter-pack.js](src/17-starter-pack.js) Рђћ NEW FILE in its own IIFE): `maybeOfferStarterPack(scoreOverride)` is the public entry Рђћ throttled 1/min internally, fetches status with the player's best score, and if `available=true` mounts a `.starter-pack-home-banner` at the TOP of `#home-screen-v2`. Banner: ­ЪјЂ swinging icon + name + perks line (`1500­Ъњј + ОАОДОЎОЪ + 3 ОЊОеОњОЋОф BP`) + live countdown pill (`РЈ░ 6ОЎ 22ОЕ`) + gold "ОцОфОЌ Рєњ" CTA + ├Ќ close. Click banner OR CTA Рєњ `showStarterPackModal(data)` Рђћ full-screen overlay with: red "ОЌОЊ-ОцОбОъОЎОф ┬и РЈ░ 6ОЎ 22ОЕ" ribbon (loss-aversion stamp), giant ­ЪјЂ icon, contents list (3 items: gems / skin / BP tiers), value calculation card showing `~2400­Ъњј` total vs `500­Ъњј` price = `ОЌОАОЏОф 79%` (anchoring psychology), giant gold "Рюе ОДОаОћ ОбОЏОЕОЎОЋ ┬и 500­Ъњј" button. Disabled state when balance insufficient: shows `­Ъњј ОЌОАОе N­Ъњј` instead. Buy Рєњ `confirm` Рєњ POST Рєњ on success: local balance + skin cache update, `soundMilestone(6)` + buzz, full-screen `showStarterPackWelcomeOverlay` (spinning ­ЪјЂ, "ОфОЋОЊОћ!", contents recap). **Trigger** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): game-over branch fires `maybeOfferStarterPack(score)` BEFORE the over-screen renders so the server can stamp eligibility with this game's score. Skipped for bot/skin-trial games. **Home mount** ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)): also fires `maybeOfferStarterPack()` 800ms after mount Рђћ so a returning player who closed the banner sees it again next session (within the 7-day window). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `­ЪјЂ Starter Pack` section under ­Ъњ░ ОЏОюОЏОюОћ tab with 4 logical groups (master + naming, pricing, trigger conditions, pack contents) + 9 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with detailed economic-math examples. Cache buster `v20260523k`, SW `bloom-v9.5`.
- РюЁ **Premium Battle Pass Рђћ stage 17 Рђћ the #1 monetization driver (May 2026)** Рђћ dual-track Battle Pass with paid premium tier Рђћ the highest-revenue feature in modern F2P (Fortnite, Apex, Genshin all use this exact pattern). **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js) migrations array): 3 new columns on `player_season_progress` (`is_premium BOOLEAN` / `premium_purchased_at TIMESTAMPTZ` / `claimed_premium_tiers JSONB`); 3 master config keys (`season_pass_premium_enabled` default `'true'` / `_price_gems` default `'1500'` / `_price_usd` default `'4.99'`); 20 premium reward keys `season_tier_<N>_premium_reward` seeded at exactly ├Ќ2 the free reward (sum ~32,000­Ъњј/season premium vs ~16,000­Ъњј free). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `buildSeasonTiers` now emits `premiumReward` per tier (falls back to `reward ├Ќ 2` when key missing). `/api/player/season/status` returns `isPremium` + `claimedPremiumTiers` + `premiumEnabled` + `premiumPriceGems` + `premiumPriceUsd`; `unclaimedCount` double-counts when premium owned (so a player who crossed tier 5 with premium and claimed nothing sees `10 ­ЪјЂ`). `/api/player/season/claim-tier` accepts new `track` field (`'free'` | `'premium'`) Рђћ gates premium claims on `is_premium=true`, dedups per-track via `claimed_premium_tiers`, returns both arrays so the client can update state. **New endpoint** `POST /api/player/season/buy-premium`: atomic balance deduct + flip `is_premium` in a single transaction (no orphan debits possible). Returns `{ok, price, newBalance}` on success or `{ok:false, reason:'insufficient_funds', price, balance}` for UI hint. Rate-limited 10/hr. Already-premium returns idempotent `{ok:false, reason:'already_premium'}`. **Client** ([src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): rewrote `renderSeasonModalBody` to dual-track layout Рђћ each tier now shows TWO buttons side-by-side (mint free + gold premium). When premium NOT owned: premium buttons render as a `.dyn-season-track-tease` (dashed gold border, "­Ъћњ +N­Ъњј") for tiers the player has already earned Рђћ **pure loss-aversion punch**. New big `.dyn-season-buy-banner` at TOP of modal with: Рюе pulsing star, title "ОЕОЊОеОњ Ою-Premium Battle Pass", subtitle showing total premium gems available, **"­ЪјЂ N­Ъњј ОЉ-M ОЊОеОњОЋОф ОЕОЏОЉОе ОЌОдОЎОф Рђћ ОъОЌОЏОЎОЮ ОюОџ!" hint** showing exactly how much value the player is leaving on the table, and a big gold "­ЪћЊ ОЕОЊОеОњ ОбОЏОЕОЎОЋ ┬и 1500­Ъњј" CTA button. New `claimSeasonTier(tierN, track, btnEl)` signature passes track to server. New `confirmAndBuyPremium(btnEl)` Рєњ JS confirm() showing price + balance + total expected gems Рєњ POST Рєњ on success: `showPremiumWelcomeOverlay()` (full-screen golden celebration card with Рюе spinning star, "Premium ОцОбОЎОю!", auto-dismiss 8s). **Surfaces**: (1) Modal "Рюе Premium" pill in header sub when owned. (2) Modal big buy banner when not owned. (3) Each tier card shows both rewards (gold one greyed/teased without premium). (4) Home tile: `<span class="home-v2-sp-prem">Рюе Premium</span>` badge next to "ОЊОеОњОћ N" when owned. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): premium master controls section above XP rates (3 keys: enabled / price_gems / price_usd) with detailed Hebrew tooltip explaining monetization rationale + ROI math; 20-tier table got a 4th column "Рюе ­Ъњј Premium" with gold-tinted input cells, auto-saves on blur/Enter; 3 new `TIPS_PER_KEY` entries with economic-math examples ("default 1500­Ъњј Рєњ returns 32,000­Ъњј = 20├Ќ ROI"). The premium track is fully toggleable Рђћ admin can disable via `season_pass_premium_enabled='false'` and the entire premium UI disappears (existing premium-owners keep their claimed rewards intact). Cache buster `v20260523j`, SW `bloom-v9.4`. **Stripe IAP wiring is stage 17b** Рђћ currently the USD price is display-only.

- РюЁ **Daily Special Board Рђћ stage 15 Рђћ daily mini-event boards (May 2026)** Рђћ the #1 daily-return hook in F2P puzzle games, ported to BLOOM. Every day at Asia/Jerusalem midnight ONE dynamic board is anointed as "­ЪїЪ ОћОюОЋОЌ ОЕОю ОћОЎОЋОЮ" with **├Ќ3 Season XP + ├Ќ2 quest rewards**. Deterministic pick Рђћ all players see the SAME board today, but it rotates. Players who play it daily get massive Season Pass acceleration; players who skip a day feel the loss. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql)): 4 new `game_config` keys Рђћ `daily_special_enabled` (master, default `'true'`) + `daily_special_xp_mult` (default `'3'`) + `daily_special_reward_mult` (default `'2'`) + `daily_special_override_id` (default `''`, lets admin force a specific board for today, e.g. Valentine on 14/2). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): new `_dailySpecialHash(dateStr)` FNV-1a hash Рєњ deterministic index into the active dynamic-boards list. `pickDailySpecial(boardRows)` is the picker, `getDailySpecialForToday()` re-queries for the XP/reward branches. `GET /api/boards/available` now returns `{ ok, boards, dailySpecial: {enabled, id, xpMult, rewardMult, date, isOverride} }` at the top level Рђћ single-fetch, no extra round trip. `POST /api/player/season/grant-xp` reads `meta.boardId` and when it matches today's special multiplies `xpGain` by `xpMult` (capped at `season_xp_max_per_game ├Ќ Math.ceil(xpMult)` so the daily can earn ~300 XP/game on default). `POST /api/player/earn` `dyn_quest` branch reads `meta.boardId` and multiplies the quest reward by `rewardMult` when the boardId matches today's special. Both are server-authoritative Рђћ client never names the multipliers. **Client** ([src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) + [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): `window._dailySpecial` populated from the same `/api/boards/available` response that already runs every 90s. New `hasPlayedDailySpecialToday(date, boardId)` + `markDailySpecialPlayed(date, boardId)` localStorage helpers keyed on the date so it auto-resets at midnight. **Surfaces**: (1) **Picker header banner** Рђћ at the ABSOLUTE TOP of the picker (above tournaments + season pass + quests): gold-pink pulsing gradient `.dyn-daily-special-banner` with ­ЪїЪ icon (rotating + scaling), board name in strong, 3 inline pills (`3├Ќ XP` mint, `2├Ќ ОцОеОАОЎОЮ` mint, `ОЕОЌОД ОбОЏОЕОЎОЋ Рєљ` gold CTA). Tap = closes picker + immediately starts the special board. (2) **Picker card glow** Рђћ the special board's card gets a `.daily-special` class with breathing gold border + box-shadow (`dailySpecialCardGlow` 2.6s keyframes), plus a unique gold-pink chip at the top of its chip row: `­ЪїЪ ОћОюОЋОЌ ОЕОю ОћОЎОЋОЮ ┬и 3├Ќ XP ┬и 2├Ќ ОцОеОАОЎОЮ`. (3) **Home button label** Рђћ new `.fomo-daily-special` class with gold-pink gradient. Inserted into the existing priority ladder: `questClaimable > streakDanger > dailySpecial-unplayed > FOMO-countdown > streak-calm > default`. When the player hasn't played today's special yet: `­ЪїЪ ОћОюОЋОЌ ОЕОю ОћОЎОЋОЮ: ОЋОюОаОўОЎОЎОЪ ┬и 3├Ќ XP ОъОЌОЏОЎОЮ!`. Auto-disappears after `markDailySpecialPlayed` fires on game-over. (4) **Game-over banner** ([src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js)) Рђћ gold-pink `.over-daily-special-banner` immediately after the rank pill (above streak/ach/quest banners) with the celebration message "­ЪїЪ ОЕОЎОЌОДОф ОљОф ОћОюОЋОЌ ОЕОю ОћОЎОЋОЮ! ┬и ОДОЎОЉОюОф **3├Ќ XP** + **2├Ќ ОцОеОАОЎОЮ** ОбОю ОћОъОЕОЌОД ОћОќОћ". CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css) with full dark-theme overrides. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): 4 new `TIPS_PER_KEY` entries with economic-math examples + 2 new `PRESETS_PER_KEY` chip lists (`daily_special_xp_mult: [1.5, 2, 3, 4, 5]` / `daily_special_reward_mult: [1.5, 2, 2.5, 3]`). The `daily_special_override_id` field stays free-text since it's a numeric board id. Cache buster `v20260523g`, SW `bloom-v9.1`.
- РюЁ **Daily Login Multiplier Stack Рђћ stage 14 Рђћ prospective FOMO via breakdown rows (May 2026)** Рђћ the existing daily-login bonus already had streak tiers (15Рєњ200­Ъњј for 1Рєњ30 day streaks), but it was a black box: the player saw `+50­Ъњј` and didn't understand why.
